= –ó–∞–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å (proxy) –æ–±–æ—Ä–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å –∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –∂–µ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å. –¶–µ–ª—å - "–ø—Ä–∏—Ç–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç—å—Å—è" –æ—Ä–∏–≥–∏–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–º –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–æ–º –∏ —Å–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—å –æ—Ç –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞ –¥–µ—Ç–∞–ª–∏. –¢–∏–ø–∏—á–Ω—ã–µ –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä—ã –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è - –ª–µ–Ω–∏–≤–∞—è –∏–Ω–∏—Ü–∏–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –æ–±–æ—Ä–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–µ–º–æ–≥–æ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∞ –∏–ª–∏ –æ–±–æ—Ä–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –≤—ã–∑–æ–≤–æ–≤ —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–µ–≥–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å–∞
= –î–µ–∫–æ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä —Ç–∞–∫–∂–µ –æ–±–æ—Ä–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å –∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –∂–µ –∏–ª–∏ —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å. –ò–Ω–æ–≥–¥–∞ –¥–µ–∫–æ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—é—Ç "—É–º–Ω—ã–º –∑–∞–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç–µ–ª–µ–º" (smart proxy). –¢.–µ. –¥–µ–∫–æ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–∏—Ç–≤–æ—Ä—è—Ç—å—Å—è –æ—Ä–∏–≥–∏–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–º –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–æ–º –∏ –ø—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä—è—Ç—å –µ–≥–æ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å. –ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä: —É –≤–∞—Å –µ—Å—Ç—å –∑–∞–º–µ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –ø—Ä—è—á–µ—Ç –≤—ã–∑–æ–≤—ã –∫ —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–µ–º—É —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å—É. –ú–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –¥–µ–∫–æ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –æ–±–æ—Ä–∞—á–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏ –∫—ç—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç—ã –≤—ã–∑–æ–≤–æ–≤. –î—Ä—É–≥–æ–π –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä: –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–∏—Ç—å —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –æ—Ä–∏–≥–∏–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∞, –Ω–æ –æ–Ω –∑–∞–∫—Ä—ã—Ç –¥–ª—è –Ω–∞—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è. –°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –¥–µ–∫–æ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä—è–µ—Ç –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å –æ—Ä–∏–≥–∏–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∞
= –ê–¥–∞–ø—Ç–µ—Ä —Ç–∞–∫–∂–µ –æ–±–æ—Ä–∞—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å, –Ω–æ –ø—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å. –¢.–µ. –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –≤ —Å–ª—É—á–∞—è—Ö, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –µ—Å—Ç—å –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å —Å –Ω—É–∂–Ω—ã–º–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ –∏ –ø–æ–≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º, –Ω–æ —Å –Ω–µ–ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥—è—â–∏–º –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä—Ñ–µ–π—Å–æ–º

| –ê–¥–∞–ø—Ç–µ—Ä     | –ò–∑–º–µ–Ω—è–µ—Ç                 | –ù–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω—è–µ—Ç                    |

CAP-—Ç–µ–æ—Ä–µ–º–∞ (—Ç–µ–æ—Ä–µ–º–∞ –ë—Ä—é–µ—Ä–∞) = consistency + availability + partitioning üîó

= —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö (consistency) ‚Äî –≤–æ –≤—Å–µ—Ö –≤—ã—á–∏—Å–ª–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö —É–∑–ª–∞—Ö –≤ –æ–¥–∏–Ω –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–∏–≤–æ—Ä–µ—á–∞—Ç –¥—Ä—É–≥ –¥—Ä—É–≥—É
= –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å (availability) ‚Äî –ª—é–±–æ–π –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å –∫ —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—ë–Ω–Ω–æ–π —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–µ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω—ã–º –æ—Ç–∫–ª–∏–∫–æ–º, –æ–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –±–µ–∑ –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏–∏, —á—Ç–æ –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—ã –≤—Å–µ—Ö —É–∑–ª–æ–≤ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã —Å–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–∞—é—Ç
= —É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—å –∫ —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é (partition tolerance) ‚Äî —Ä–∞—Å—â–µ–ø–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—ë–Ω–Ω–æ–π —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –∏–∑–æ–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Å–µ–∫—Ü–∏–π –Ω–µ –ø—Ä–∏–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç –∫ –Ω–µ–∫–æ—Ä—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –æ—Ç–∫–ª–∏–∫–∞ –æ—Ç –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–π –∏–∑ —Å–µ–∫—Ü–∏–π

= –í —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–µ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∞ CA –≤–æ –≤—Å–µ—Ö —É–∑–ª–∞—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã –∏ –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–∞ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å, –ø—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º –æ–Ω–∞ –∂–µ—Ä—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç —É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—å—é –∫ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∞–¥—É –Ω–∞ —Å–µ–∫—Ü–∏–∏. –¢–∞–∫–∏–µ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω—ã –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ —Ç–µ—Ö–Ω–æ–ª–æ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏—è, –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–≤–∞—é—â–µ–≥–æ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –≤ —Å–º—ã—Å–ª–µ ACID, –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä–∞–º–∏ —Ç–∞–∫–∏—Ö —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º –º–æ–≥—É—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω—ã—Ö —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –±–∞–∑–∞–º–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∏–ª–∏ —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—ë–Ω–Ω–∞—è —Å–ª—É–∂–±–∞ –∫–∞—Ç–∞–ª–æ–≥–æ–≤ LDAP
= –°–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∞ CP –≤ –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–π –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç —Ü–µ–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω—ã–π —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç –∏ —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±–Ω–∞ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤ —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–∏—è—Ö —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∞–¥–∞, –Ω–æ –¥–æ—Å—Ç–∏–≥–∞–µ—Ç —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –≤ —É—â–µ—Ä–± –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏: –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –Ω–µ –≤—ã–¥–∞–≤–∞—Ç—å –æ—Ç–∫–ª–∏–∫ –Ω–∞ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å. –£—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç—å –∫ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∞–¥—É –Ω–∞ —Å–µ–∫—Ü–∏–∏ —Ç—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥—É–±–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–π –≤–æ –≤—Å–µ—Ö —É–∑–ª–∞—Ö —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã, –≤ —Å–≤—è–∑–∏ —Å —ç—Ç–∏–º –æ—Ç–º–µ—á–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∞—è —Ü–µ–ª–µ—Å–æ–æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –≤ —Ç–∞–∫–∏—Ö —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞—Ö —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—ë–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –ø–µ—Å—Å–∏–º–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏—Ö –±–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä–æ–≤–æ–∫ –¥–ª—è —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è —Ü–µ–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏
= –í —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–µ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∞ AP –Ω–µ –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è —Ü–µ–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å, –Ω–æ –ø—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω—ã —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–∏—è –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –∏ —É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –∫ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–∞–¥—É –Ω–∞ —Å–µ–∫—Ü–∏–∏. –•–æ—Ç—è —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã —Ç–∞–∫–æ–≥–æ —Ä–æ–¥–∞ –∏–∑–≤–µ—Å—Ç–Ω—ã –∑–∞–¥–æ–ª–≥–æ –¥–æ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø–∞ CAP (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—ë–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤–µ–±-–∫—ç—à–∏ –∏–ª–∏ DNS), —Ä–æ—Å—Ç –ø–æ–ø—É–ª—è—Ä–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–π —Å —ç—Ç–∏–º –Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä–æ–º —Å–≤–æ–π—Å—Ç–≤ —Å–≤—è–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Å —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º —Ç–µ–æ—Ä–µ–º—ã CAP. –¢–∞–∫, –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–æ NoSQL-—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ –Ω–µ –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä—É—é—Ç —Ü–µ–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –∏ —Å—Å—ã–ª–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ —Ç–µ–æ—Ä–µ–º—É CAP –∫–∞–∫ –Ω–∞ –º–æ—Ç–∏–≤ —Ç–∞–∫–æ–≥–æ –æ–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–∏—è. –ó–∞–¥–∞—á–µ–π –ø—Ä–∏ –ø–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–µ–Ω–∏–∏ AP-—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∏—Ç—Å—è –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–µ–∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ —Ü–µ–ª–µ—Å–æ–æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–Ω–æ–≥–æ —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω—è —Ü–µ–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –≤ —ç—Ç–æ–º —Å–º—ã—Å–ª–µ –ø—Ä–æ AP-—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä—è—Ç –∫–∞–∫ –æ ¬´—Ü–µ–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω—ã—Ö –≤ –∫–æ–Ω–µ—á–Ω–æ–º –∏—Ç–æ–≥–µ¬ª (eventually consistent) –∏–ª–∏ –∫–∞–∫ –æ ¬´—Å–ª–∞–±–æ —Ü–µ–ª–æ—Å—Ç–Ω—ã—Ö¬ª (weak consistent)

= BASE (Basically Available, Soft-state, Eventually consistent ‚Äî –±–∞–∑–æ–≤–∞—è –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å, –Ω–µ—É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–æ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ, —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –≤ –∫–æ–Ω–µ—á–Ω–æ–º —Å—á—ë—Ç–µ)
= –ü–æ–¥ –±–∞–∑–æ–≤–æ–π –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑—É–º–µ–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è —Ç–∞–∫–æ–π –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥ –∫ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—é –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã —Å–±–æ–π –≤ –Ω–µ–∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö —É–∑–ª–∞—Ö –ø—Ä–∏–≤–æ–¥–∏–ª –∫ –æ—Ç–∫–∞–∑—É –≤ –æ–±—Å–ª—É–∂–∏–≤–∞–Ω–∏–∏ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –¥–ª—è –Ω–µ–∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–π —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏ —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏–π –ø—Ä–∏ —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –≤ –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–µ —Å–ª—É—á–∞–µ–≤.
= –ù–µ—É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–æ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ–¥—Ä–∞–∑—É–º–µ–≤–∞–µ—Ç –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∂–µ—Ä—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –¥–æ–ª–≥–æ–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏—è —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏–π (—Ç–∞–∫–∏—Ö –∫–∞–∫ –ø—Ä–æ–º–µ–∂—É—Ç–æ—á–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç—ã –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä–æ–∫, –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—è –æ –Ω–∞–≤–∏–≥–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç–µ), –ø—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º –∫–æ–Ω—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä—É—è—Å—å –Ω–∞ —Ñ–∏–∫—Å–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–∏—á–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–π.
= –°–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –≤ –∫–æ–Ω–µ—á–Ω–æ–º —Å—á—ë—Ç–µ, —Ç—Ä–∞–∫—Ç—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –∫–∞–∫ –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–∏–≤–æ—Ä–µ—á–∏–≤–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –≤ –Ω–µ–∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö —Å–ª—É—á–∞—è—Ö, –Ω–æ –ø—Ä–∏ –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –≤ –ø—Ä–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –æ–±–æ–∑—Ä–∏–º–æ–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è.

IoC vs DI üîó
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/6550700/inversion-of-control-vs-dependency-injection
IoC (Inversion of Control) - is generic term and implemented in several ways (events, delegates etc).
Giving control to the container to get an instance of the object is called IoC, means instead of you are creating an object using the new operator, let the container do that for you
DI (Dependency Injection) - DI is a sub-type of IoC and is implemented by constructor injection, setter injection or Interface injection.
Spring supports only Constructor Injection and Setter/Getter Injection.

–ü—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ–≤–∏—Å–ª–æ (–≤—Ä–æ–¥–µ –±—ã), –∫–∞–∫ —É–±–µ–¥–∏—Ç—å—Å—è –≤ —ç—Ç–æ–º –∏ —á—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –¥–∞–ª—å—à–µ? üîó
–ü–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤ (–ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–æ—Ä–∞, –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏) –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º, –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –≥–¥–µ-—Ç–æ —É–ø–µ—Ä–ª–æ—Å—å –≤ –æ–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–∏—è
–ü–æ–¥–∫–ª—é—á–∏—Ç—å—Å—è –ø–æ JMX, –ø–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å –º–µ—Ç—Ä–∏–∫–∏ JVM —Å —ç—Ç–æ–π –∂–µ —Ü–µ–ª—å—é
–°–Ω—è—Ç—å —Ö–∏–ø–¥–∞–º–ø/—Ç—Ä–µ–¥–¥–∞–º–ø, —Å–∫–∞—á–∞—Ç—å –µ–≥–æ, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –ø—Ä–æ–∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å

–û—Ç–ª–∏—á–∏–µ ReentrantLock –æ—Ç synchronized üîó
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/11821801/why-use-a-reentrantlock-if-one-can-use-synchronizedthis
A ReentrantLock is unstructured, unlike synchronized constructs - so you don't need to use a block structure for locking and can even hold a lock across methods.
Aside from that, ReentrantLock supports lock polling and interruptible lock waits that support time-out, and support for configurable fairness policy, allowing more flexible thread scheduling.
When should you use ReentrantLocks? The answer is pretty simple - use it when you actually need something it provides that synchronized doesn't, like timed lock waits, interruptible lock waits, non-block-structured locks, multiple condition variables, or lock polling.

–¶–∏–∫–ª –∂–∏–∑–Ω–∏ —Å–ø—Ä–∏–Ω–≥-–±–∏–Ω–∞, –∫–∞–∫ –≤—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—å—Å—è –≤ –Ω–µ–≥–æ? üîó
https://www.journaldev.com/2637/spring-bean-life-cycle
= By implementing InitializingBean and DisposableBean interfaces ‚Äì Both these interfaces declare a single method where we can initialize/close resources in the bean. For post-initialization, we can implement InitializingBean interface and provide implementation of afterPropertiesSet() method. For pre-destroy, we can implement DisposableBean interface and provide implementation of destroy() method.
This approach is simple to use but it‚Äôs not recommended because it will create tight coupling with the Spring framework in our bean implementations.
= Providing init-method and destroy-method attribute values for the bean in the spring bean configuration file.
This is the recommended approach because of no direct dependency to spring framework and we can create our own methods.
Note that both post-init and pre-destroy methods should have no arguments but they can throw Exceptions. We would also require to get the bean instance from the spring application context for these methods invocation.
= Spring framework also support @PostConstruct and @PreDestroy annotations for defining post-init and pre-destroy methods. These annotations are part of javax.annotation package. However for these annotations to work, we need to configure our spring application to look for annotations. We can do this either by defining bean of type org.springframework.context.annotation.CommonAnnotationBeanPostProcessor or by context:annotation-config element in spring bean configuration file.
= All of the *Aware interfaces are sub-interfaces of Aware and declare a single setter method to be implemented by the bean:
= ApplicationContextAware ‚Äì to inject ApplicationContext object, example usage is to get the array of bean definition names.
= BeanFactoryAware ‚Äì to inject BeanFactory object, example usage is to check scope of a bean.
= BeanNameAware ‚Äì to know the bean name defined in the configuration file.
= ResourceLoaderAware ‚Äì to inject ResourceLoader object, example usage is to get the input stream for a file in the classpath.
= ServletContextAware ‚Äì to inject ServletContext object in MVC application, example usage is to read context parameters and attributes.
= ServletConfigAware ‚Äì to inject ServletConfig object in MVC application, example usage is to get servlet config parameters.

What's new in latest Javas: 8-12? üîó

Java 8 üîó
https://habr.com/ru/post/216431/
= lambda expressions (closures). lambda expression corresponds to functional interface
= multiple new functional interfaces:
== Predicates: functions which take one argument and return boolean
== Functions: take one argument and return result
== Consumers: operation on one input argument
== Comparators: some new methods was added: reversed(), comparingInt(), comparingLong() etc
= Optional: allow to prevent NPE
= default methods in interfaces
= Nashorn JS engine
= new Date and Time API: Clock, ZoneId, LocalTime, LocalDate, LocalDateTime, DateTimeFormatter
= links to methods and constructors, for example: String::valueOf, Person::new
= Streams (sequential and parallel): sequence of elements on which we could perform different operations. two types of operations:
== intermediate: Filter, Sorted, Map
== terminal: Match (return boolean), Count (return long), Reduce (return Optional)
= new methods in Map: putIfAbsent(), computeIfPresent(), computeIfAbsent(), getOrDefault(), merge()
= annotations became repeatable
= CompletableFuture with about 50 different methods for composing, combining, executing asynchronous computation steps and handling errors

Java 9-11: https://codete.com/blog/java-8-java-11-quick-guide/

Java 9 üîó
= Project Jigsaw: introduced modularity to monolithic Java SE ecosystem. The primary goal to make JDK more easily scalable down to small computing devices. Using module-info.java files we could declare which part of module we could expose
= JShell: provides REPL - interactive programming tool
= G1 garbage collector that introduced in Java 8 became default GC instead previous Parallel GC
= private methods in interfaces
= new methods in Optional class: ifPresentOrElse(), or()
= Optional.stream(): Can treat with Optional as a Stream and use all methods from Stream API
= static methods on the List, Set and Map interfaces for creating unmodifiable instances of those collections
= new methods to CompletableFuture class. Most significant one relates to timeouts, for example: orTimeout(), completeOnTimeout()
= enhancements in @Deprecated, added 2 new params to it: 'since' and 'forRemoval'

Java 10 üîó
= "var" keyword introduced. It allows to replace strict variable type declaration if the type may be easily inferred by the compiler.
We can use var in the context of local variables (instantly initialized), for loops and try-with-resources blocks.
= new overloaded version of Optional.orElseThrow() without params which throws NoSuchElementException dy default
= API for creating unmodifiable collections from existing collections: List.copyOf(), Set.copyOf(), Map.copyOf()
= Collectors class has some new methods like toUnmodifiableList(), toUnmodifiableSet(), toUnmodifiableMap()
= Parallel full GC for G1: G1 which was introduced in Java 9 and mainly designed to prevent "stop the world" event in this Java improved the algorithm to parallelize the full GC

Java 11 üîó
https://habr.com/ru/post/424683/
= Local-Variable Syntax for Lambda Parameters, for example: (var x) -> x * 2. So could use 'var' here already
= Add single-file programs support. Typing simply: 'java SimpleProgram.java' will run the program immediately.
Support of "shebang files" added too: put '#!/usr/bin/java --source 11' into the first line of .java file for that
= HTTP client API introduced in Java 9 as incubator project now became a part of Java SE standard
= some modules removed from standard Java SE (corba, transaction, activation, xml.ws, xml.bind, xml.ws.annotation)
= multiple new methods in public API: String, Pattern, Predicate, Path, Files etc
= new optional Epsilon GC which doesn't collect garbage at all (useful for serverless usage, short-term tasks etc when guaranteed that heap will be enough and JVM should not collect statistics to decide when GC should start)
= Flight Recorder became not-comercial and already presents in OpenJDK too
= Nashorn as replacement of Rhino Javascript engine

Java 12 üîó
https://www.baeldung.com/java-12-new-features
= String class 2 new methods: indent (add or remove spaces at the start of each line) and transform (accept one function parameter and applies it to the string)

= new Files::mismatch method - compare two files and find the position of the first mismatched byte in their contents. The return value will be in the inclusive range of 0L up to the byte size of the smaller file or -1L if the files are identical.

= A new teeing collector was introduced:

Collector<T, ?, R> teeing(Collector<? super T, ?, R1> downstream1, Collector<? super T, ?, R2> downstream2, BiFunction<? super R1, ? super R2, R> merger)
It is a composite of two downstream collectors. Every element is processed by both downstream collectors. Then their results are passed to the merge function and transformed into the final result.

= New number formatter ‚Äì the CompactNumberFormat. It's designed to represent a number in a shorter form, based on the patterns provided by a given locale.
The format style can be either SHORT or LONG. For a better understanding of the format styles, let's consider number 1000 in the US locale. The SHORT style would format it as ‚Äú10K‚Äù, and the LONG one would do it as ‚Äú10 thousand‚Äù.

NumberFormat likesShort = NumberFormat.getCompactNumberInstance(new Locale("en", "US"), NumberFormat.Style.SHORT);
likesShort.setMaximumFractionDigits(2);
assertEquals("2.59K", likesShort.format(2592));

NumberFormat likesLong = NumberFormat.getCompactNumberInstance(new Locale("en", "US"), NumberFormat.Style.LONG);
likesLong.setMaximumFractionDigits(2);
assertEquals("2.59 thousand", likesShort.format(2592));

= Preview changes (could be switched on by separate flag):
== Switch Expressions (Preview)

String typeOfDay = switch (dayOfWeek) {
    case MONDAY, TUESDAY, WEDNESDAY, THURSDAY, FRIDAY -> {
		// more logic
		System.out.println("Working Day")
    };
    case SATURDAY, SUNDAY -> "Day Off";
};

== Pattern Matching for instanceof (Preview)

if (obj instanceof String s) {
    // no explicit cast needed
    int length = s.length();
}
The compiler will automatically inject the typecasted String s variable for us.

== JVM changes
=== Shenandoah: A Low-Pause-Time Garbage Collector
Shenandoah is an experimental garbage collection (GC) algorithm, for now not included in the default Java 12 builds.
It reduces the GC pause times by doing evacuation work simultaneously with the running Java threads. This means that with Shenandoah, pause times are not dependent on the heap‚Äôs size and should be consistent. Garbage collecting a 200 GB heap or a 2 GB heap should have a similar low pause behavior.
Shenandoah will become part of mainline JDK builds since version 15.

=== Microbenchmark Suite
Java 12 introduces a suite of around 100 microbenchmark tests to the JDK source code.
These tests will allow for continuous performance testing on a JVM and will become useful for every developer wishing to work on the JVM itself or create a new microbenchmark.

=== Default CDS Archives
The Class Data Sharing (CDS) feature helps reduce the startup time and memory footprint between multiple Java Virtual Machines. It uses a built-time generated default class list that contains the selected core library classes.
The change that came with Java 12 is that the CDS archive is enabled by default. To run programs with CDS turned off we need to set the Xshare flag to off:
Java -Xshare:off HelloWorld.java

https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SQL_window_function
https://mode.com/sql-tutorial/sql-window-functions/
In the SQL, window functions allow access to data in the records right before and after the current record. A window function defines a frame or window of rows with a given length around the current row, and performs a calculation across the set of data in the window. For example next query extracts for each row the values of a window with one preceding and one following row:

SELECT
	LAG(name,1) OVER(ORDER BY name) "prev",
	name, 
	LEAD(name,1) OVER(ORDER BY name) "next"
	FROM people ORDER BY name

List of windows functions: SUM(),COUNT(),AVG(),ROW_NUMBER(),RANK(),DENSE_RANK(),NTILE(),LAG(),LEAD()
To narrow the window from the entire dataset to individual groups within the dataset, you can use PARTITION BY.
To write several window functions into the same query, using the same window, you can create an alias using WINDOW:

SELECT
	LAG(name,1) OVER name_window "prev",
	name, 
	LEAD(name,1) OVER name_window "next"
	FROM people 
	WINDOW name_window AS (PARTITION BY country ORDER BY name)
	ORDER BY name

Hot/cold DB storages üîó
https://searchstorage.techtarget.com/definition/hot-data
Hot data is data that needs to be accessed frequently. It is typically business-critical information that needs to be accessed quickly and is often used by a company for quick decision making (computation). Hot data usually resides on the fastest storage - typically flash in hybrid or tiered storage environments.
Conversely, cool data is data that is accessed less frequently by an organization. Cool data is usually stored on lower performing and less expensive storage environments in-house or in the cloud.

= –ü–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–∑–±–∏–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü, —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞—â–∏—Ö –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–µ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–µ–π, –Ω–∞ –ª–æ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–µ —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –ø–æ –Ω–µ–∫–∏–º –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º –∞–¥–º–∏–Ω–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–º –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∏—è–º. –ü–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü –¥–µ–ª–∏—Ç –≤–µ—Å—å –æ–±—ä–µ–º –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–π –ø–æ –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –Ω–µ–∑–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏–º—ã—Ö –∏ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–ª–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è—é—â–∏—Ö—Å—è –ø–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–≤, —á—Ç–æ —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —É—Å–∫–æ—Ä—è–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—É –°–£–ë–î. –î–ª—è –ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏–ª—å–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥—É—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–æ–≤ –ø–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º–æ, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –≤ –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–º –ø–æ—Ç–æ–∫–µ –±—ã–ª–æ –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä–Ω–æ –æ–¥–∏–Ω–∞–∫–æ–≤–æ–µ –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–µ–π.
–ù–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, –Ω–∞ –Ω–æ–≤–æ—Å—Ç–Ω—ã—Ö —Å–∞–π—Ç–∞—Ö –∏–º–µ–µ—Ç —Å–º—ã—Å–ª –ø–∞—Ä—Ç–∏—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∏ –ø–æ –¥–∞—Ç–µ –ø—É–±–ª–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏, —Ç–∞–∫ –∫–∞–∫ —Å–≤–µ–∂–∏–µ –Ω–æ–≤–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–∫–æ–≤ –±–æ–ª–µ–µ –≤–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã –∏ —á–∞—â–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç—Å—è —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞ –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Å –Ω–∏–º–∏, –∞ –Ω–µ —Å–æ –≤—Å–µ–º –∞—Ä—Ö–∏–≤–æ–º –∑–∞ –≥–æ–¥—ã —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –Ω–æ–≤–æ—Å—Ç–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–∞.

= –†–µ–ø–ª–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –∏–ª–∏ –∞—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –∫–æ–ø–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –º–µ–∂–¥—É –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–∏–º–∏ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞–º–∏. –í–µ–¥—É—â–∏–µ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞ –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—é—Ç –º–∞—Å—Ç–µ—Ä–∞–º–∏ (master), –∞ –≤–µ–¥–æ–º—ã–µ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞ ‚Äî —Å–ª—ç–π–≤–∞–º–∏ (slave). –ú–∞—Å—Ç–µ—Ä–∞ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—é—Ç—Å—è –¥–ª—è –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –∞ —Å–ª—ç–π–≤—ã ‚Äî –¥–ª—è —Å—á–∏—Ç—ã–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è. –í –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–π —Å—Ö–µ–º–µ —Ä–µ–ø–ª–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ –æ–¥–∏–Ω –º–∞—Å—Ç–µ—Ä –∏ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Å–ª—ç–π–≤–æ–≤, —Ç–∞–∫ –∫–∞–∫ –≤ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ–π —á–∞—Å—Ç–∏ –≤–µ–±-–ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–æ–≤ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–π —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏—è –Ω–∞ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–∫–æ–≤ –±–æ–ª—å—à–µ, —á–µ–º –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–π –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∏.
–ù–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–∏—Ö –¥–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö slave-—Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–æ–≤ –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç —Å–Ω—è—Ç—å —Å –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞ –Ω–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫—É –∏ –ø–æ–≤—ã—Å–∏—Ç—å –æ–±—â—É—é –ø—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã, –∞ —Ç–∞–∫–∂–µ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å —Å–ª—ç–π–≤—ã –ø–æ–¥ –∫–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω—ã–µ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ—ë–º–∫–∏–µ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á–∏ –∏ —Ç–∞–∫–∏–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–º, –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, —É–ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—å —Å–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Å–µ—Ä—å—ë–∑–Ω—ã—Ö –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏—Ö –æ—Ç—á—ë—Ç–æ–≤ ‚Äî –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ–º—ã–π –¥–ª—è —ç—Ç–∏—Ö —Ü–µ–ª–µ–π slave –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å –Ω–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–µ–Ω –Ω–∞ 100%, –Ω–æ –Ω–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—É –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏—Ö –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–≤–ª–∏—è–µ—Ç.

= –®–∞—Ä–¥–∏–Ω–≥ ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∏–µ–º, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—è—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –º–µ–∂–¥—É —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã–º–∏ —Ñ–∏–∑–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–º–∏ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞–º–∏. –ü—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å —à–∞—Ä–¥–∏–Ω–≥–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø–æ–ª–∞–≥–∞–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–∑–Ω–µ—Å–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –º–µ–∂–¥—É –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–º–∏ —à–∞—Ä–¥–∞–º–∏ –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ –Ω–µ–∫–æ–≥–æ –∫–ª—é—á–∞ —à–∞—Ä–¥–∏–Ω–≥–∞. –°–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –æ–¥–∏–Ω–∞–∫–æ–≤—ã–º –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º –∫–ª—é—á–∞ —à–∞—Ä–¥–∏–Ω–≥–∞ —Å—É—â–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –≥—Ä—É–ø–ø–∏—Ä—É—é—Ç—Å—è –≤ –Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –ø–æ –∑–∞–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–º—É –∫–ª—é—á—É, –∞ —ç—Ç–æ—Ç –Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—Å—è –≤ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ö –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Ñ–∏–∑–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–æ–≥–æ —à–∞—Ä–¥–∞. –≠—Ç–æ —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –æ–±–ª–µ–≥—á–∞–µ—Ç –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫—É –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö.

= –ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–µ—Ç –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω—ã–µ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω—ã–µ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å—ã, –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã–º (Bootstrap –∏–ª–∏ Primordial), –∫–æ—Ä–Ω–µ–≤—ã–º –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫–æ–º –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–æ–≤. –ò–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –æ–Ω –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–µ—Ç –≤–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–∏–µ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å—ã JDK –∏ –ø–∞–∫–µ—Ç—ã java.* (rt.jar –∏ i18n.jar). –£–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–æ–π –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã—Ö –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–æ–≤ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å—é –∫–ª—é—á–∞ -Xbootclasspath, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç –ø–µ—Ä–µ–æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—è—Ç—å –Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä—ã –±–∞–∑–æ–≤—ã—Ö –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–æ–≤.
= –ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫ —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–π ‚Äì –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–µ –ø–∞–∫–µ—Ç—ã —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–π, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ —Ä–∞—Å–ø–æ–ª–∞–≥–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –≤ –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∏ /lib/ext –∏–ª–∏ –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π –¥–∏—Ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∏, –æ–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–π –≤ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω–æ–º –ø–∞—Ä–∞–º–µ—Ç—Ä–µ java.ext.dirs. –≠—Ç–æ –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –Ω–æ–≤—ã–µ —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–∏—è –±–µ–∑ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –º–æ–¥–∏—Ñ–∏—Ü–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π–∫–∏ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ–º—ã—Ö –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–π. –£–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–æ–π —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–π –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å—é —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω–æ–π –æ–ø—Ü–∏–∏ java.ext.dirs.
= –°–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω—ã–π –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫ ‚Äì –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–µ—Ç –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å—ã, –ø—É—Ç–∏ –∫ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–º —É–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω—ã –≤ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π –æ–∫—Ä—É–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è CLASSPATH –∏–ª–∏ –ø—É—Ç–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ —É–∫–∞–∑–∞–Ω—ã –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –∫–ª—é—á–µ–π ‚Äìclasspath –∏–ª–∏ ‚Äìcp. –¢–∞–∫–∂–µ —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å —Å–ø–∏—Å–∫–æ–º –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–æ–≤ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–Ω–æ–π –æ–ø—Ü–∏–µ–π java.class.path.
–ö–∞–∂–¥—ã–π –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–æ–≤ (–∫—Ä–æ–º–µ Bootstrap) –∏–º–µ–µ—Ç —Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å–∫–∏–π –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å —É–∂–µ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–ª—Å—è —Ä–∞–Ω–µ–µ —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–∏–º –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫–æ–º - –æ–Ω –≤–æ–∑–≤—Ä–∞—â–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∏–∑ –∫–µ—à–∞. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ—Ç - –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫ –¥–µ–ª–µ–≥–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–∞ —Ä–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å–∫–æ–º—É –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å—É-–∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫—É. Bootstrap –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫ - –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–µ—Ç –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å —Å–∞–º–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –±—É—Ç—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–ø –Ω–µ –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å –¥–ª—è –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ - —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–æ –ø–æ –∏–µ—Ä–∞—Ä—Ö–∏–∏ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—ã–¥—É—â–µ–º—É –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫—É –∏ —Ç.–¥.:

1.2) –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ–Ω, –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∞ –¥–µ–ª–µ–≥–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫—É —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–π.
2) –ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑—á–∏–∫ —Ä–∞—Å—à–∏—Ä–µ–Ω–∏–π –ø–æ–ø—ã—Ç–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å –≤ –∫–µ—à–µ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å Student.

= –û–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏—Å—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∞—è –±–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∞ –Ω–µ –æ–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –º–æ–¥–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ–±—Ä–∞–±–∞—Ç—ã–≤–∞–µ–º—ã—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–∏–º–∏ —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏—è–º–∏, –æ–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–æ–º –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø–æ–ª–∞–≥–∞–µ–º–æ–π –º–æ–¥–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–µ–∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–≥–æ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∞—Ç—Ä–∏–±—É—Ç–∞ –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–π –∏–∑ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö (–æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞–∏–º–µ–Ω–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ VERSION –∏ —Ü–µ–ª–æ—á–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ç–∏–ø —Å –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–º –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º 0). –ü–µ—Ä–µ–¥ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å—é –º–æ–¥–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–π –≤ –±–∞–∑—É –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∞—Ç—Ä–∏–±—É—Ç–∞, –∏ –µ—Å–ª–∏ –æ–Ω–æ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª–æ—Å—å, —Ç–æ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏—è –æ—Ç–∫–∞—Ç—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∏–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è—é—Ç—Å—è —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–µ —Å—Ö–µ–º—ã —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ–ª–ª–∏–∑–∏–π. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∞—Ç—Ä–∏–±—É—Ç–∞ –Ω–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª–æ—Å—å ‚Äî –ø—Ä–æ–∏–∑–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è —Ñ–∏–∫—Å–∞—Ü–∏—è –º–æ–¥–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–π —Å –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∞—Ç—Ä–∏–±—É—Ç–∞ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, –∏–Ω–∫—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–º) –¥–ª—è —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–º —Å–µ—Å—Å–∏—è–º –æ —Ç–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–∏–ª–∏—Å—å. –ö–æ–Ω–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ –∫–æ–¥–∞ —ç—Ç–æ —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∞ —Å where VERSION=... .

–ù–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–π–∫–∞ —Å–±–æ—Ä—â–∏–∫–∞ –º—É—Å–æ—Ä–∞ üîó
https://dzone.com/articles/choosing-the-right-gc
Java -XX:+Use[gc_name]GC -Xmx2g -Xms32m -jar app.jar [sleep]
Where params are next:
= [gc_name] will be substituted with the specific garbage collector type: G1, Parallel, ConcMarkSweep (CMS), Serial, Shenandoah etc
= Xms is the scaling step (32 MB in our case)
= Xmx is the maximum scaling limit (2 GB in our case)
= [sleep] is the interval between memory load cycles in milliseconds. The default is 10
From plot in this article we see that Parallel GC not released memory to OS when it not used already
To choose appropriate GC we need to track memory consumption of live application and experiment with different GCs and their options. In addition optimal settings depend on how fast memory usage growth is

= –ù–∞ –±–∞–∑–µ Windows - –≤–∏—Ä—Ç—É–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞—è –º–∞—à–∏–Ω–∞ —Å Linux, –≥–¥–µ —É–∂–µ –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç chroot (—Å–º. –≤—ã—à–µ).

–°–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∏–∑–æ–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –æ–∫—Ä—É–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–æ–≤ –∏ –Ω–∞ —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ —Å–µ—Ç–∏, –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –º—ç–ø–ø–∏–Ω–≥ –ø–æ—Ä—Ç–æ–≤ –∏ –º–∞—É–Ω—Ç–∏—Ç—å volumes, –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å—ã –≤ –Ω–æ–≤—ã—Ö –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ö (docker run), –æ—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä—ã (docker stop –∏ docker start), –ø—Ä–∏–æ—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏ –≤–æ–∑–æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å—ã –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä–∞—Ö (docker pause –∏ docker unpause), –æ—Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –º–æ–Ω–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–Ω–≥ –∑–∞–ø—É—â–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–æ–≤ (docker ps –ø–æ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–æ–≥–∏–∏ —Å ps –≤ Unix-—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞—Ö, docker top –ø–æ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–æ–≥–∏–∏ —Å top –∏ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–µ). –ù–æ–≤—ã–µ –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑—ã –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏–∑ —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–Ω–æ–≥–æ —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞ (docker build, —Ñ–∞–π–ª —Å—Ü–µ–Ω–∞—Ä–∏—è –Ω–æ—Å–∏—Ç –Ω–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ Dockerfile), –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å –≤—Å–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è, —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä–µ, –≤ –Ω–æ–≤—ã–π –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑ (docker commit).
–ú–æ–∂–Ω–æ –≤–∑–∞–∏–º–æ–¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å —Å –ø—É–±–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–º —Ä–µ–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–µ–º Docker Hub, –≤ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–º —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—â–µ–Ω—ã –ø—Ä–µ–¥–≤–∞—Ä–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å–æ–±—Ä–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑—ã –∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä–æ–≤, –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–∞ docker search –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç –æ—Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç—å –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫ –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–≤ —Å—Ä–µ–¥–∏ —Ä–∞–∑–º–µ—â—ë–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –≤ –Ω—ë–º.
–û–±—Ä–∞–∑—ã –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å–∫–∞—á–∏–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤ –ª–æ–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω—É—é —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—É (docker pull), –∏–ª–∏ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –ª–æ–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å–æ–±—Ä–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑—ã –≤ Docker Hub (docker push).
–¢–∞–∫–∂–µ Docker –∏–º–µ–µ—Ç –ø–∞–∫–µ—Ç–Ω—ã–π –º–µ–Ω–µ–¥–∂–µ—Ä Docker Compose, –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—é—â–∏–π –æ–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å –∏ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ–∫–æ–Ω—Ç–µ–π–Ω–µ—Ä–Ω—ã–µ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è.

Sql-–∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å—ã —Å –∞–≥—Ä–µ–≥–∞—Ç–Ω—ã–º–∏ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è–º–∏ üîó

–ê–≥—Ä–µ–≥–∞—Ç–Ω—ã–µ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—é—Ç—Å—è –¥–ª—è –æ–±–æ–±—â–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö. –ö –∏—Ö —á–∏—Å–ª—É –æ—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—è—Ç—Å—è:

MAX(–º–∞–∫—Å–∏–º–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–µ –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ)

MODE (–º–æ–¥–∞)
MEDIAN (–º–µ–¥–∏–∞–Ω–∞)
–ü—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä: SELECT SUM(amt) FROM Orders WHERE odate BETWEEN '2016-01-01' and '2016-12-31';

–ö–∞–∫ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç lazy –≤ jpa –ø–æ–¥ –∫–∞–ø–æ—Ç–æ–º üîó
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/2990799/difference-between-fetchtype-lazy-and-eager-in-java-persistence-api
FetchType.LAZY = fetch when needed
FetchType.EAGER = fetch immediately
This is implemented by creating a Proxy around the List (or Set). So for your lazy collections, the concrete types are not ArrayList and HashSet, but PersistentSet and PersistentList (or PersistentBag).

–ü—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ n+1 üîó
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/97197/what-is-the-n1-selects-problem-in-object-relational-mapping
When you have 1-to-may relationship, for example collection of Car objects (database rows) where each Car has a collection of Wheel objects (also rows)
You need to iterate through all the cars, and for each one, print out a list of the wheels. The naive O/R implementation would do the following: SELECT * FROM Cars.
And then for each Car: SELECT * FROM Wheel WHERE CarId = ?
In other words, you have one select for the Cars, and then N additional selects, where N is the total number of cars.
How to solve N+1 problem:
https://dou.ua/lenta/articles/hibernate-fetch-types/
–ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—è —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–µ FetchMode, –Ω–∞—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–∏–≤–∞–µ–º –∫–∞–∫ –º—ã —Ö–æ—Ç–∏–º, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å—É—â–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –∏–ª–∏ –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –±—ã–ª–∏ –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–µ–Ω—ã:
= SELECT ‚Äî –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—è –ø–æ –¥–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–º—É SQL –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å—É –Ω–∞ –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–∫—Ü–∏—é,
= JOIN ‚Äî –≤ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–º –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–µ —Å –∫–æ—Ä–Ω–µ–≤–æ–π —Å—É—â–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—è SQL –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–æ—Ä JOIN,
= SUBSELECT‚Äî –≤ –¥–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–º –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–µ, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—è SUBSELECT.
–ú—ã —Ç–∞–∫–∂–µ –º–æ–∂–µ–º –≤–ª–∏—è—Ç—å –Ω–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏—é –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–∫—Ü–∏–π –ø—Ä–∏ –ø–æ–º–æ—â–∏ –∞–Ω–Ω–æ—Ç–∞—Ü–∏–∏ @BatchSize (–∏–ª–∏ –∞—Ç—Ä–∏–±—É—Ç batch-size –≤ XML), –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ –∫–æ–ª–ª–µ–∫—Ü–∏–π, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –±—É–¥—É—Ç –∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –≤ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–º –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–µ.

Ehcache üîó

Ehcache ‚Äî —É–Ω–∏–≤–µ—Ä—Å–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞—è —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—ë–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–µ—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑—É–µ—Ç –∫–µ—à –∫–∞–∫ –¥–∏–Ω–∞–º–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏–π (–≤ –æ–ø–µ—Ä–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ–π –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏), —Ç–∞–∫ –∏ –¥–∏—Å–∫–æ–≤—ã–π –∫–µ—à, –ø—Ä–∏—á—ë–º –∏–∑–Ω–∞—á–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ —Å–ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–∞—è –¥–ª—è —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã —Å –∫–µ—à–∞–º–∏ –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–≥–æ –æ–±—ä—ë–º–∞ (–ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–∫–∞ –≥–∏–≥–∞–±–∞–π—Ç–æ–≤) –∏ –≤ —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—ë–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞—Ö.
Ehcache –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ä–∞–∑–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã—Ö —Å—Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–µ–≥–∏–π –∫–µ—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è, –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä ‚Äî LFR (–∫–µ—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥—è –∏–∑ —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ—Ç—ã –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è) –∏–ª–∏ FIFO, –∞ —Ç–∞–∫–∂–µ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ç—Ä–æ–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –∫–µ—à –Ω–∞ —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ–≤ (–∑–∞–¥–∞–≤–∞—è —Å—Ö–µ–º—É –∏–Ω–≤–∞–ª–∏–¥–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ–≤ –≤ –∫–µ—à–µ ‚Äî –ø–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –∂–∏–∑–Ω–∏ –∏–ª–∏ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è).
–û–¥–Ω–æ–π –∏–∑ —É–Ω–∏–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–π ehcache —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è ¬´–ø–µ—Ä—Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–Ω—ã–π –∫–µ—à¬ª, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ–≤ –¥–∞–∂–µ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–∑–∞–≥—Ä—É–∑–∫–∏ –≤–∏—Ä—Ç—É–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π java-–º–∞—à–∏–Ω—ã. –ö—Ä–æ–º–µ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ, —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ –∫–µ—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø–æ–¥–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª—å —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è JMX, —á—Ç–æ –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–∑—Ä–∞—á–Ω–æ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –µ—ë –≤ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—É —É–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –ª—é–±—ã–º –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—è —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç–Ω—ã–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–ª—ã –∏ –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏.
–°–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –∏/–∏–ª–∏ —Ä–µ–ø–ª–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—è –∫–µ—à–µ–π –º–µ–∂–¥—É —É–∑–ª–∞–º–∏ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å –∫–∞–∫ –æ–±—â–µ–π, —Ç–∞–∫ –∏ –ª–æ–∫–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π, –¥–ª—è –æ—Ç–¥–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö –∫–µ—à–µ–π –ø–æ —Å–≤–æ–µ–π —Å—Ö–µ–º–µ, –∞—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–π –∏–ª–∏ —Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–π. –î–ª—è –±–æ–ª—å—à–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–∞ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –æ—Ç –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—é—â–µ–≥–æ –∫–µ—à, —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –Ω–∏—á–µ–≥–æ –Ω–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–±—É–µ—Ç—Å—è, –≤—Å–µ –∑–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ—Ç –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥—É—Ä–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ XML —Ñ–∞–π–ª–∞.
–ö–µ—à –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å –∫–∞–∫ —Å–∞–º–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–π –µ–¥–∏–Ω–∏—Ü–µ–π –≤ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–µ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è, —Ç–∞–∫ –∏ –≤–∑–∞–∏–º–æ–¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å —Å –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–º–∏ –ø–æ–ø—É–ª—è—Ä–Ω—ã–º–∏ —Ñ—Ä–µ–π–º–≤–æ—Ä–∫–∞–º–∏, –≤ —á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏, —Å –ø—Ä–æ—Å–ª–æ–π–∫–æ–π –¥–ª—è —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã —Å –±–∞–∑–∞–º–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö Hibernate.

–§–µ—Ç—á-—Ç–∞–π–ø/–º–æ–¥, —Å–∞–±—Å–µ–ª–µ–∫—Ç üîó
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/25821718/difference-between-fetchmode-and-fetchtype
https://www.solidsyntax.be/2013/10/17/fetching-collections-hibernate/
FetchType (Lazy/Eager) tells whether we want entity to be loaded eagerly or lazy, when there's call in code.
FetchMode (Select/Join) tells whether we want our entity to be loaded with additional select or in one query with join or subselect.
a) if you don't specify FetchMode, the default is JOIN and FetchType works normal
b) if you specify FetchMode.JOIN explicitly, FetchType is ignored and a query is always eager
c) if you specify FetchMode.SELECT or FetchMode.SUBSELECT, FetchType.Type works normal
What mode choose: select or join:
https://stackoverflow.com/questions/617145/hibernate-fetching-strategy-when-to-use-join-and-when-to-use-select
Join is supposed to solve the n+1 problem. The join method is a little less efficient on the initial query because you're duplicating the parent columns in every row, but you only make one round-trip to the database.
Select:

	SELECT * FROM parent WHERE id=(whatever)
	SELECT * FROM child WHERE id=(parent.child.id)
Join:
	SELECT * FROM parent
	LEFT OUTER JOIN child ON parent.child.id=child.id
	WHERE parent.id=(whatever)

–†–∞—Å—Å–∫–∞–∑–∞—Ç—å –æ jms (connection, session, producer, consumer) üîó

JMS, Java Message Service - API –¥–ª—è —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã —Å message oriented middleware, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–≤–∞—Ç—å –≥–∏–±–∫–∏–µ –∏ —Å–ª–∞–±–æ—Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º –∞—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –æ–±–º–µ–Ω–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏ –º–µ–∂–¥—É –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è–º–∏ (–∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–º–∏/—Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞–º–∏) —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ –ø–æ—Å—Ä–µ–¥–Ω–∏–∫–∞. –ê—Å–∏–Ω—Ö—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å - –∏ –µ—Å—Ç—å –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–Ω–∞—è –ø—Ä–∏—á–∏–Ω–∞ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è JMS.

Spring bean vs factory bean üîó
http://www.geekabyte.io/2014/11/difference-between-beanfactory-and.html
A FactoryBean is an interface that you implements when writing factory classes and you want the object created by the factory to be managed as a bean by Spring,
A BeanFactory represents the Spring IoC container, it contains the managed beans and provides access to retrieving them. It is part of the core of the framework which implements the base functionality of an inversion of control container.
In more succinct words, the BeanFactory represents the Spring container while the FactoryBean represents factory classes whose created object are picked up and registered as a bean in the container.

Iterator: fail-fast vs fail-safe üîó
https://www.baeldung.com/java-fail-safe-vs-fail-fast-iterator
= Fail-fast iterators in Java don‚Äôt play along when the underlying collection gets modified.
Collections maintain an internal counter called modCount. Each time an item is added or removed from the Collection, this counter gets incremented.
When iterating, on each next() call, the current value of modCount gets compared with the initial value. If there‚Äôs a mismatch, it throws ConcurrentModificationException which aborts the entire operation.
Default iterators for Collections from java.util package such as ArrayList, HashMap, etc. are Fail-Fast.
The ConcurrentModificationException gets thrown at the beginning of a next iteration cycle after the modification was performed.
= Fail-Safe iterators favor lack of failures over the inconvenience of exception handling.
Those iterators create a clone of the actual Collection and iterate over it. If any modification happens after the iterator is created, the copy still remains untouched. Hence, these Iterators continue looping over the Collection even if it‚Äôs modified.
However, it‚Äôs important to remember that there‚Äôs no such thing as a truly Fail-Safe iterator. The correct term is Weakly Consistent.
That means, if a Collection is modified while being iterated over, what the Iterator sees is weakly guaranteed. This behavior may be different for different Collections and is documented in Javadocs of each such Collection.
The Fail-Safe Iterators have a few disadvantages, though. One disadvantage is that the Iterator isn‚Äôt guaranteed to return updated data from the Collection, as it‚Äôs working on the clone instead of the actual Collection.
Another disadvantage is the overhead of creating a copy of the Collection, both regarding time and memory.
Iterators on Collections from java.util.concurrent package such as ConcurrentHashMap, CopyOnWriteArrayList, etc are Fail-Safe in nature.

OAuth 2 –ø—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç —Å–æ–±–æ–π —Ñ—Ä–µ–π–º–≤–æ—Ä–∫ –¥–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—é—â–∏–π –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è–º –æ—Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –æ–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –∫ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å–∫–∏–º –∞–∫–∫–∞—É–Ω—Ç–∞–º –Ω–∞ HTTP —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å–∞—Ö.
–û–Ω —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –ø–æ –ø—Ä–∏–Ω—Ü–∏–ø—É –¥–µ–ª–µ–≥–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è —Å–µ—Ä–≤–∏—Å—É, –Ω–∞ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–º –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è –∞–∫–∫–∞—É–Ω—Ç –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è, –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—è —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–Ω–µ–º—É –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—é –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞—Ç—å –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –∫ –∞–∫–∫–∞—É–Ω—Ç—É –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è.

= –í–ª–∞–¥–µ–ª–µ—Ü —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–∞
–í–ª–∞–¥–µ–ª—å—Ü–µ–º —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–∞ —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑—É–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–ª—è –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞ –∫ —Å–≤–æ–µ–º—É –∞–∫–∫–∞—É–Ω—Ç—É. –î–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å–∫–æ–º—É –∞–∫–∫–∞—É–Ω—Ç—É –æ–≥—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—á–µ–Ω "–æ–±–ª–∞—Å—Ç—å—é –≤–∏–¥–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏" (scope) –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –ø—Ä–∞–≤ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ (–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –Ω–∞ —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏–ª–∏ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å).

= –°–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤
–°–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤ –Ω–µ–ø–æ—Å—Ä–µ–¥—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç –∑–∞—â–∏—â—ë–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∞–∫–∫–∞—É–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–π, –∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ—Ç –ø–æ–¥–ª–∏–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–º, –∞ –∑–∞—Ç–µ–º —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—ë—Ç –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω—ã –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è, —Å –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å—é –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –æ—Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –∫ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å—Å–∫–∏–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º.

= –ö–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç
–ö–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–º —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–µ —Ö–æ—á–µ—Ç –æ—Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç—å –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –∫ –∞–∫–∫–∞—É–Ω—Ç—É –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è. –ü–µ—Ä–µ–¥ –æ—Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–æ –±—ã—Ç—å –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ–º, –∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–∞ –±—ã—Ç—å –æ–¥–æ–±—Ä–µ–Ω–∞ —Å–æ —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã API.

= –ê–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä

–ü–æ—Ä—è–¥–æ–∫ –≤–∑–∞–∏–º–æ–¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—è:
1. –ü—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç —É –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é –Ω–∞ –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø –∫ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä—É —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤.
2. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑—É–µ—Ç –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å, –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é (authorization grant).
3. –ü—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω —É —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ (API) –ø—É—Ç—ë–º –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏—è –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –æ —Å–∞–º–æ–º —Å–µ–±–µ –∏ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –Ω–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ—Ç –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è.
4. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –ø–æ–¥–ª–∏–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∞ –∏ —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—é –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ, —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ (API) —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—ë—Ç —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞ –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è. –ü—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à—ë–Ω.
5. –ü—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å —É —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞ —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤ (API), –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è—è –ø—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω –¥–æ—Å—Ç—É–ø–∞ –¥–ª—è –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏.
6. –ï—Å–ª–∏ —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª–µ–Ω, —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤ (API) –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –∑–∞–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞–µ–º—ã–π —Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—é.

OpenID üîó

OpenID ‚Äî –æ—Ç–∫—Ä—ã—Ç—ã–π —Å—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç –¥–µ—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–π —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è—é—â–µ–π –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—é –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –µ–¥–∏–Ω—É—é —É—á—ë—Ç–Ω—É—é –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å –¥–ª—è –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –Ω–∞ –º–Ω–æ–∂–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ –Ω–µ —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –¥—Ä—É–≥ —Å –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–º –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω–µ—Ç-—Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å–æ–≤, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—è —É—Å–ª—É–≥–∏ —Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å–∏—Ö –ª–∏—Ü.
–ë–∞–∑–æ–≤–æ–π —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–µ–π OpenID —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–æ—Ä—Ç–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω–æ–≥–æ, –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç-–æ—Ä–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ, —Ü–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤–æ–≥–æ –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∞ –¥–ª—è —Å–≤–æ–±–æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏ –¥–µ—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è.
–ù–∞ —Å–∞–π—Ç–µ, –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, example.com –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞ –≤—Ö–æ–¥–∞ —Å –µ–¥–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º –ø–æ–ª–µ–º –≤–≤–æ–¥–∞ –¥–ª—è OpenID –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∞. –ó–∞—á–∞—Å—Ç—É—é —Ä—è–¥–æ–º —Å —Ç–∞–∫–∏–º –ø–æ–ª–µ–º —Ä–∞—Å–ø–æ–ª–∞–≥–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –ª–æ–≥–æ—Ç–∏–ø OpenID. –î–ª—è —Ç–æ–≥–æ, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –Ω–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–º —Å–∞–π—Ç–µ —Å –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å—é —Å–≤–æ–µ–≥–æ –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä–∞, –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, pupkin.openid-provider.org, –∑–∞—Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ —É OpenID –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ openid-provider.org, –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—é –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º–æ –≤–≤–µ—Å—Ç–∏ —Å–≤–æ–π –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –≤ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–∞–≥–∞–µ–º—É—é –Ω–∞ —Å–∞–π—Ç–µ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º—É –≤—Ö–æ–¥–∞. –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ —Å–∞–π—Ç example.com –ø–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è –Ω–∞ —Å–∞–π—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞. –°–∞–π—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç —É –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è –ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–∂–¥–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –ª–∏ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å –∂–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ —Å–≤–æ–µ–π —É—á—ë—Ç–Ω–æ–π –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å–∏. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å —Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—à–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è, —Ç–æ —Å–∞–π—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ —Å–∞–π—Ç –∑–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏–º–æ–π —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω—ã. –ü—Ä–∏ –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–Ω–æ–º –ø–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—Å—Ç –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª–µ –∑–∞–≤–∏—Å–∏–º–æ–π —Å—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–Ω–µ.
OpenID –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—é –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –æ–¥–Ω—É —É—á–µ—Ç–Ω—É—é –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—å, –∑–∞—Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—É—é —É OpenID –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞, –Ω–∞ –º–Ω–æ–∂–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏—Ö —Å–∞–π—Ç–æ–≤. –ü–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –≤—ã–±—Ä–∞—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫—É—é –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –ø—Ä–µ–¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Å–∞–π—Ç—É.
–°—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –¥–µ–ª–µ–≥–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è OpenID.
–°–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞ OpenID ‚Äî –¥–µ—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–∞—è —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–∞. –≠—Ç–æ –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç, —á—Ç–æ –Ω–µ—Ç –∫–∞–∫–æ–π-–ª–∏–±–æ —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π —Å–ª—É–∂–±—ã –∏–ª–∏ –æ—Ä–≥–∞–Ω–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è —Ä–∞–∑—Ä–µ—à–∞–ª–∞ –±—ã –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã –∏–ª–∏ —Ä–µ–≥–∏—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–ª–∞ –±—ã –∑–∞–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞—é—â–∏–µ –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏—é OpenID –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–Ω–µ—Ç-—Ä–µ—Å—É—Ä—Å—ã –∏–ª–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–æ–≤ OpenID. –ö–æ–Ω–µ—á–Ω—ã–π –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç —Å–≤–æ–±–æ–¥–Ω–æ –≤—ã–±–∏—Ä–∞—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–∞–π–¥–µ—Ä–∞ OpenID –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å.

JWT üîó

–ü—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ—Ç JWT –¥–ª—è –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∏ –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—è —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–º:
1. –°–ø–µ—Ä–≤–∞ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å –∑–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –Ω–∞ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —Å –ø–æ–º–æ—â—å—é –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–ª—é—á–∞ (—ç—Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å –ø–∞—Ä–∞ –ª–æ–≥–∏–Ω/–ø–∞—Ä–æ–ª—å, –ª–∏–±–æ Facebook –∫–ª—é—á, –ª–∏–±–æ Google –∫–ª—é—á, –ª–∏–±–æ –∫–ª—é—á –æ—Ç –¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π —É—á–µ—Ç–∫–∏).
2. –ó–∞—Ç–µ–º —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–µ—Ç JWT –∏ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –µ–≥–æ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—é.
3. –ö–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å –∫ API –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è, –æ–Ω –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –∫ –Ω–µ–º—É –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π —Ä–∞–Ω–µ–µ JWT.
4. –ü—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å –ø–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–º—É —Å –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–æ–º JWT, —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ª–∏ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å —Ç–µ–º, –∑–∞ –∫–æ–≥–æ —Å–µ–±—è –≤—ã–¥–∞–µ—Ç. –í —ç—Ç–æ–π —Å—Ö–µ–º–µ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è —Å–∫–æ–Ω—Ñ–∏–≥—É—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω —Ç–∞–∫, —á—Ç–æ —Å–º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å, —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ª–∏ –≤—Ö–æ–¥—è—â–∏–π JWT –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Ç–µ–º, —á—Ç–æ –±—ã–ª —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–æ–º –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏.
JWT —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ–∏—Ç –∏–∑ —Ç—Ä–µ—Ö —á–∞—Å—Ç–µ–π: –∑–∞–≥–æ–ª–æ–≤–æ–∫ header, –ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ payload –∏ –ø–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å—å signature.
= –•–µ–¥–µ—Ä JWT —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏—Ç –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ —Ç–æ–º, –∫–∞–∫ –¥–æ–ª–∂–Ω–∞ –≤—ã—á–∏—Å–ª—è—Ç—å—Å—è JWT –ø–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å—å.
= Payload ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ –ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ —Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—è—Ç—Å—è –≤–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–∏ JWT. –≠—Ç–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Ç–∞–∫–∂–µ –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—é—Ç JWT-claims (–∑–∞—è–≤–∫–∏).
= Signature –≤—ã—á–∏—Å–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—ã–¥—É—â–∏—Ö –¥–≤—É—Ö –ø–æ–ª–µ–π. –ê–ª–≥–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–º base64url –∫–æ–¥–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç header –∏ payload, —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –Ω–∞ 1 –∏ 2 —à–∞–≥–µ. –ó–∞–∫–æ–¥–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∏ —Å–æ–µ–¥–∏–Ω—è—é—Ç—Å—è —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ —Ç–æ—á–∫—É, –∑–∞—Ç–µ–º –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∞ —Ö–µ—à–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç—Å—è –∞–ª–≥–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–º–æ–º, –∑–∞–¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º –≤ —Ö–µ–¥–µ—Ä–µ –Ω–∞ –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–µ –Ω–∞—à–µ–≥–æ —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∫–ª—é—á–∞.
–í–∞–∂–Ω–æ –ø–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞—Ç—å, —á—Ç–æ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ JWT –ù–ï —Å–∫—Ä—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç –∏ –Ω–µ –º–∞—Å–∫–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –∞–≤—Ç–æ–º–∞—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏. –ü—Ä–∏—á–∏–Ω–∞, –ø–æ—á–µ–º—É JWT –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—é—Ç—Å—è ‚Äî —ç—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞, —á—Ç–æ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –±—ã–ª–∏ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω—ã –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º –∏—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫–æ–º. –ö–∞–∫ –±—ã–ª–æ –ø—Ä–æ–¥–µ–º–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–æ –≤—ã—à–µ, –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –≤–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–∏ JWT –∑–∞–∫–æ–¥–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã –∏ –ø–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å–∞–Ω—ã, –æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç–∏—Ç–µ –≤–Ω–∏–º–∞–Ω–∏–µ, —ç—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –æ–¥–Ω–æ –∏ —Ç–æ–∂–µ, —á—Ç–æ –∑–∞—à–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã.
–ü—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∫–∞ JWT. –¢–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –∏ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–Ω–∞—é—Ç —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω—ã–π –∫–ª—é—á. –°–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∞–µ—Ç —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω—ã–π –∫–ª—é—á –æ—Ç —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞ –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –≤–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∫–∏ –∞—É—Ç–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–æ–≤. –ü–æ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫—É –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∑–Ω–∞–µ—Ç —Å–µ–∫—Ä–µ—Ç–Ω—ã–π –∫–ª—é—á, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç API-–∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å —Å –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º –∫ –Ω–µ–º—É —Ç–æ–∫–µ–Ω–æ–º, –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç—å —Ç–æ—Ç –∂–µ –∞–ª–≥–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–º –ø–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –∫ JWT, —á—Ç–æ –≤ —à–∞–≥–µ 3. –ü—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–∏—Ç—å —ç—Ç—É –ø–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å—å, —Å—Ä–∞–≤–Ω–∏–≤–∞—è –µ–µ —Å–æ —Å–≤–æ–µ–π —Å–æ–±—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π, –≤—ã—á–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π —Ö–µ—à–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –ø–æ–¥–ø–∏—Å–∏ —Å–æ–≤–ø–∞–¥–∞—é—Ç, –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç JWT –≤–∞–ª–∏–¥–Ω—ã–π, —Ç.–µ. –ø—Ä–∏—à–µ–ª –æ—Ç –ø—Ä–æ–≤–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏—Å—Ç–æ—á–Ω–∏–∫–∞.

–ü—Ä–æ—Ñ–∞–π–ª–∏–Ω–≥ JVM üîó

CPU: time/calls, sampling
= Wall clock time/calls. –ë—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–æ, –ø—Ä—è–º–æ –≤ –∫–æ–¥–µ, —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–µ–π currentTimeMillis(); –Ω–æ –æ–Ω–∞ –Ω–µ —Ç–æ—á–Ω–∞—è, –º–µ—Ä—è–µ—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≤ –º—Å–µ–∫
= Short/fast calls. –ï—Å—Ç—å –≤–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –Ω–∞—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã–π –∫–æ–¥, —Å–ª–∏–Ω–∫–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å —Å –∂–∞–≤–∞-–∫–æ–¥–æ–º –∏ —Ç–∞–∫ –∏–∑–º–µ—Ä—è—Ç—å
= Sampling. –î–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å —Ç—Ä–µ–¥–¥–∞–º–ø—ã –∏ —Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å, –≤ –∫–∞–∫–∏—Ö –º–µ—Å—Ç–∞—Ö –∑–∞—Å—Ç–∞–µ–º –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º—É —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ. –ï—Å–ª–∏ —É –≤–∞—Å –≤ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–µ –µ—Å—Ç—å —Å—Ç—Ä–æ—á–∫–∞, –≤ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–π –æ–Ω–∞ —Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–∏—Ç –≤—Å–µ, –∏–ª–∏ –ø–æ –∫—Ä–∞–π–Ω–µ–π –º–µ—Ä–µ 90% —Å–≤–æ–µ–≥–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏, –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, –∫–∞–∫–æ–π-–Ω–∏–±—É–¥—å —Ü–∏–∫–ª, –∞ —Ç–∞–º, –≤ –≥–ª—É–±–∏–Ω–µ, –∫–∞–∫–∞—è-—Ç–æ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ—á–∫–∞, —Ç–æ —Å–∫–æ—Ä–µ–µ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ, –ø—Ä–∏ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∫–µ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤—ã –µ–µ –≤ —ç—Ç–æ–π —Å—Ç—Ä–æ—á–∫–µ –∏ –∑–∞—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–µ—Ç–µ. –¢–∞–∫–æ–µ –º–µ—Å—Ç–æ –≤ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–µ –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è "–≥–æ—Ä—è—á–µ–π —Ç–æ—á–∫–æ–π". –≠—Ç–æ –≤—Å–µ–≥–¥–∞ –∑–∞–º–µ—á–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∫–∞–Ω–¥–∏–¥–∞—Ç –¥–ª—è –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏. –ß—Ç–æ –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–Ω–æ ‚Äî –µ—Å—Ç—å –≤—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–µ–Ω–Ω–∞—è —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏—è –ø–æ–¥ –Ω–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º "thread dump", —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å –¥–∞–º–ø –≤—Å–µ—Ö –ø–æ—Ç–æ–∫–æ–≤. –í Windows –æ–Ω–∞ –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø—É—Ç–µ–º –Ω–∞–∂–∞—Ç–∏—è CTRL-Break –Ω–∞ –∫–æ–Ω—Å–æ–ª–∏, –∞ –Ω–∞ Linux –∏ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏—Ö —é–Ω–∏–∫—Å–∞—Ö —ç—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ—Å—ã–ª–∫–æ–π —Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å–µ–≥–æ —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞–ª–∞, –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥–æ–π "kill -3".
–¢–∞–∫–∂–µ –≤ —Å–æ–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö Java-–º–∞—à–∏–Ω–∞—Ö –µ—Å—Ç—å –∑–∞–º–µ—á–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–∞—è —É—Ç–∏–ª–∏—Ç–∞ jstack, –µ–π –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥–∞—Ç—å –∏–¥–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–æ—Ä –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–∞, –∏ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å –Ω–∞ –≤—ã—Ö–æ–¥–µ thread dump.
–°–¥–µ–ª–∞–π—Ç–µ –Ω–µ –æ–¥–∏–Ω thread dump, —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–π—Ç–µ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ thread dump–æ–≤. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –Ω–∏—á–µ–≥–æ –Ω–µ –≤—ã–ª–æ–≤–∏—Ç, –ø–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏—Ç–µ –µ—â–µ –Ω–∞ –ø–∞—Ä—É-—Ç—Ä–æ–π–∫—É. –ú–æ–∂–µ—Ç —É –≤–∞—Å –≤ –≥–æ—Ä—è—á–µ–π —Ç–æ—á–∫–µ –Ω–µ —Å—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç, –∞ 50%.
–≠—Ç—É –∏–¥–µ—é –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Ä–∞–∑–≤–∏—Ç—å –¥–∞–ª—å—à–µ. –ú–æ–∂–Ω–æ, –∑–∞–ø—É—Å—Ç–∏–≤ JVM, –ø–µ—Ä–µ–Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å –µ–µ –≤—ã—Ö–æ–¥ –≤ —Ñ–∞–π–ª, –∏ –∑–∞–ø—É—Å—Ç–∏—Ç—å —Å–∫—Ä–∏–ø—Ç, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç thread dump –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–µ —Ç—Ä–∏ —Å–µ–∫—É–Ω–¥—ã. –≠—Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —Å–ø–æ–∫–æ–π–Ω–æ –Ω–∞ –∂–∏–≤–æ–π —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–µ, –±–µ–∑ –∫–∞–∫–æ–≥–æ –ª–∏–±–æ —Ä–∏—Å–∫–∞ —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ —Å –Ω–µ–π —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å. –ü–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ —Å–∞–º —Å–±–æ—Ä thread dump –¥–æ—Å—Ç–∞—Ç–æ—á–Ω–æ –±—ã—Å—Ç—Ä–∞—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ–¥—É—Ä–∞, –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—Ç –æ—Ç —Å–∏–ª—ã 100 –º–∏–ª–ª–∏—Å–µ–∫—É–Ω–¥, –¥–∞–∂–µ –ø—Ä–∏ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –±–æ–ª—å—à–æ–º –∫–æ–ª–∏—á–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–¥–æ–≤. –¢.–µ. —ç—Ç–æ —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–Ω–æ –±–µ–∑–æ–ø–∞—Å–Ω—ã–π –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç –ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –∂–∏–≤—ã—Ö –∏ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—â–∏—Ö —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º. –ü–æ—Å–ª–µ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ, –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏–≤ —Ñ–∞–π–ª thread dump, –µ–≥–æ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ø–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å –≥–ª–∞–∑–∫–∞–º–∏, –∞ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –Ω–∞–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å –Ω–µ—Å–ª–æ–∂–Ω—ã–π –∫—É—Å–æ–∫ –∫–æ–¥–∞, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç, —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ-–Ω–∏–±—É–¥—å —Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—Å—Ç–∏–∫–∏ ‚Üí —Ö–æ—Ç—è –±—ã —Ç—É–ø–æ, –ø–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥—ã –ø—Ä–æ—è–≤–∏–ª–∏—Å—å –∏ —Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ä–∞–∑, –ø–æ—Å–º–æ—Ç—Ä–µ—Ç—å, –≤ –∫–∞–∫–æ–º —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–∏ –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏–ª–∏—Å—å –ø–æ—Ç–æ–∫–∏.
= Integration. –ë–æ–ª–µ–µ —Ç–æ–≥–æ, thread dump –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –≤ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è, –≤ Java –µ—Å—Ç—å –∑–∞–º–µ—á–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –º–µ—Ç–æ–¥ Thread.getAllStackTraces, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è–µ—Ç –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ stacktrace –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–Ω–æ. –¢–∞–∫–∏–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–º, –≤—ã –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ–≥—Ä–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ, –∫–∞–∫ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—É—é —á–∞—Å—Ç—å —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è, –∏ —Ä–∞—Å–ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω—è—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ –≤–∞—à–∏–º –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–º, —Å —É–∂–µ –≤—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º –ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º. –¢–µ–º —Å–∞–º—ã–º, —É –≤–∞—Å –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –ø–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–Ω—ã–π –ø–æ—Ç–æ–∫ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –≤—ã —Å–º–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –¥–ª—è —É–ª—É—á—à–µ–Ω–∏—è –≤–∞—à–µ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è.
Memory: usage, allocation
= Usage. –ï—Å—Ç—å –æ—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–π –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç jmap, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç –≥–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º—É —Ç–æ–≥–æ, —á–µ–º —É –≤–∞—Å –∑–∞–±–∏—Ç–∞ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç—ã –∏ —Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏ –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞—é—Ç. –≠—Ç–æ –∑–∞–º–µ—á–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–π –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç –¥–ª—è –æ–±—â–µ–≥–æ –æ–±–∑–æ—Ä–∞, —á—Ç–æ –∂–µ —É –≤–∞—Å –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç, –∏ —á–µ–º –∑–∞–±–∏—Ç–∞ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç—å. –ü—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ –≤ —Ç–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ –≤—ã —Ç–∞–∫–∏–º –æ–±—Ä–∞–∑–æ–º –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç–µ –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ –≤—Å–µ—Ö –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç–∞—Ö, –¥–∞–∂–µ —Ç–µ—Ö, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ —Å–µ–π—á–∞—Å –≤ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–π –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç –Ω–µ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—é—Ç—Å—è, –Ω–∞—Ö–æ–¥—è—Ç—Å—è –≤ –º—É—Å–æ—Ä–µ. –ü–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É —É jmap –µ—Å—Ç—å —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω–∞—è –æ–ø—Ü–∏—è 'live', –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è –ø–µ—Ä–µ–¥ —Ç–µ–º, –∫–∞–∫ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å –≥–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º—É –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç —Å–±–æ—Ä–∫—É –º—É—Å–æ—Ä–∞, –æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ–º—ã–µ –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç—ã, –∏ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç –≥–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º—É. –ü—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞, —á—Ç–æ —É–∂–µ —Å —ç—Ç–æ–π –æ–ø—Ü–∏–µ–π, –±–æ–ª—å—à—É—é, –∂–∏–≤—É—é —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—É —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—â—É—é —Å –º–Ω–æ–≥–∏–º–∏ –≥–∏–≥–∞–±–∞–π—Ç–∞–º–∏ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏, –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –Ω–µ–ª—å–∑—è, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ —Å–±–æ—Ä–∫–∞ –º—É—Å–æ—Ä–∞ —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º—ã, —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—é—â–µ–π —Å –¥–µ—Å—è—Ç–∫–æ–º –≥–∏–≥–∞–±–∞–π—Ç –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏ –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—Ç –¥–µ—Å—è—Ç–æ–∫-–¥—Ä—É–≥–æ–π —Å–µ–∫—É–Ω–¥, –∏ —ç—Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å –Ω–µ–ø—Ä–∏–µ–º–ª–µ–º–æ.
–¢–∞–∫–∂–µ –¥–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–æ –∑–Ω–∞—Ç—å –¥–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –æ–ø—Ü–∏–∏ Java-–º–∞—à–∏–Ω. –ù–∞–ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä, —É Java-–º–∞—à–∏–Ω –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ø–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç—å –æ—Ç–ø–µ—á–∞—Ç–∞—Ç—å –≥–∏—Å—Ç–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º—É –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å–æ–≤, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –≤—ã –¥–µ–ª–∞–µ—Ç–µ thread dump ‚Üí "PrintClassHistogram".
JVM –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ø–æ–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∏—Ç—å –ø—Ä–∏ –∏—Å—á–µ—Ä–ø–∞–Ω–∏–∏ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏ –∑–∞–ø–∏—Å—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å —Å–≤–æ–µ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–∞ –¥–∏—Å–∫. –≠—Ç–æ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å –ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–æ, –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º—É —á—Ç–æ –æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ, –ª—é–¥–∏ –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞—é—Ç –æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø–æ—Ç—Ä–µ–±–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ç–æ–≥–¥–∞, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –æ–Ω–∞ –∑–∞–∫–∞–Ω—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ—á–µ–º—É-—Ç–æ. –ù–∏–∫—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –∑–∞–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø—Ä–æ—Ñ–∏–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º, –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –≤—Å–µ —Ö–æ—Ä–æ—à–æ, –∞ –≤–æ—Ç –∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–µ –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞–µ—Ç –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏ –Ω–µ —Ö–≤–∞—Ç–∞—Ç—å, –æ–Ω–∞ –≤—ã–ª–µ—Ç–∞–µ—Ç, –Ω–∞—á–∏–Ω–∞—é—Ç –¥—É–º–∞—Ç—å, –∫–∞–∫ –±—ã —Ç–∞–∫ —Å–æ–ø—Ç–∏–º–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å. –ü–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É —ç—Ç–æ –æ–ø—Ü–∏—é –ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–æ –≤—Å–µ–≥–¥–∞ –∏–º–µ—Ç—å –≤–∫–ª—é—á–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–π. –¢–æ–≥–¥–∞ –≤ –ø–ª–æ—Ö–æ–º —Å–ª—É—á–∞–µ JVM –≤–∞–º –∑–∞–ø–∏—à–µ—Ç –±–∏–Ω–∞—Ä–Ω—ã–π –¥–∞–º–ø, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –≤—ã –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç–µ –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º, –Ω–µ –Ω–∞ –∂–∏–≤–æ–π —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–µ, –ª—é–±—ã–º–∏ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–º–µ–Ω—Ç–∞–º–∏ –ø—Ä–æ–∞–Ω–∞–ª–∏–∑–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å. –ü—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º, —ç—Ç–æ—Ç –¥–∞–º–ø –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –≤ –ª—é–±–æ–π –º–æ–º–µ–Ω—Ç –≤–∑—è—Ç—å —Å JVM, —Ç–µ–º –∂–µ jmap-–æ–º, —Å –æ–ø—Ü–∏–µ–π '-dump', –Ω–æ —ç—Ç–æ, –æ–ø—è—Ç—å –∂–µ, –æ—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–∞–≤–ª–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç JVM –Ω–∞ –¥–æ–ª–≥–æ–µ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è, –Ω–∞ –∂–∏–≤–æ–π —Å–∏—Å—Ç–µ–º–µ –≤—ã —ç—Ç–æ –≤—Ä—è–¥ –ª–∏ –∑–∞—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å.
= Allocation. C–º–æ—Ç—Ä–∏—Ç–µ, –Ω–∞ —Ç–æ, —Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –≤–∞—à–µ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ç—Ä–∞—Ç–∏—Ç –Ω–∞ —Å–±–æ—Ä–∫—É –º—É—Å–æ—Ä–∞. –≠—Ç–æ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å —Å–∏–≥–Ω–∞–ª–æ–º, —á—Ç–æ –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏ —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–∞–º—è—Ç—å, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è –ø–æ—Ç–æ–º –ø–µ—Ä–µ—Å—Ç–∞–µ—Ç –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è - –∏ –∫–æ–¥ –º–æ–∂–Ω–æ –ø–µ—Ä–µ–ø–∏—Å–∞—Ç—å —Ç–∞–∫, —á—Ç–æ–±—ã –∏–∑–±–µ–∂–∞—Ç—å —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ. –≠—Ç–æ –ø–æ–ª–µ–∑–Ω–∞—è –æ–ø—Ü–∏—è '-verbose:gc', '+PrintGC', '+PrintGCDetails', –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –ø–æ–∑–≤–æ–ª—è—Ç –≤–∞–º —Ä–∞–∑–æ–±—Ä–∞—Ç—å—Å—è, —Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏ –≤–∞—à–µ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–∏–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è —É—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –Ω–∞ —Å–±–æ—Ä–∫—É –º—É—Å–æ—Ä–∞. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –≤—ã –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç–µ, —á—Ç–æ –Ω–∞ —Å–±–æ—Ä–∫—É –º—É—Å–æ—Ä–∞ —É—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ–Ω—Ç –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–∏, –∑–Ω–∞—á–∏—Ç –≤—ã –≥–¥–µ-—Ç–æ –≤ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–µ –º–Ω–æ–≥–æ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª—è–µ—Ç–µ –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏, –≤—ã —ç—Ç–æ –º–µ—Å—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ—Ç–µ, –Ω—É–∂–Ω–æ –∏—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å, –∫—Ç–æ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª—è–µ—Ç –ø–∞–º—è—Ç—å. –ö–∞–∫ –∏—Å–∫–∞—Ç—å? –ï—Å—Ç—å –≤—Å—Ç—Ä–æ–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π –≤ Java-–º–∞—à–∏–Ω—É —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–±, –∫–ª—é—á–∏–∫ '-Xaprof'. –û–Ω –≤–∞–º, –∫ —Å–æ–∂–∞–ª–µ–Ω–∏—é, —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø—Ä–∏ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–∞, –≤—ã–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç —Ç–∞–∫ –Ω–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞–µ–º—ã–π allocation profile, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –≥–æ–≤–æ—Ä–∏—Ç –Ω–µ –æ —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∏–º–æ–º –ø–∞–º—è—Ç–∏, –∞ –æ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—Å—Ç–∏–∫–µ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª—è–µ–º—ã—Ö –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç–æ–≤ ‚Üí –∫–∞–∫–∏–µ –æ–±—ä–µ–∫—Ç—ã –∏ –∫–∞–∫ —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª—è–ª–∏—Å—å. –ï—Å–ª–∏ —É –≤–∞—Å —ç—Ç–æ –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç, –≤—ã —Å–∫–æ—Ä–µ–µ –≤—Å–µ–≥–æ —É–≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç–µ, —á—Ç–æ –≥–¥–µ-—Ç–æ –∑–∞–≤–µ–¥–µ–Ω –∫–∞–∫–æ–π-—Ç–æ –≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–π –∫–ª–∞—Å—Å, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –¥–µ–π—Å—Ç–≤–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ –æ—á–µ–Ω—å —á–∞—Å—Ç–æ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è. –ü–æ–ø—Ä–æ–±—É–π—Ç–µ —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å 'aprof' ‚Äî –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –≤—ã —Å—Ä–∞–∑—É –Ω–∞–π–¥–µ—Ç–µ –≤–∞—à—É –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—É. –ê —á—Ç–æ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å, –µ—Å–ª–∏ —É –≤–∞—Å –Ω–µ—Ç –∏–¥–µ–∏, –≥–¥–µ —ç—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–æ–∏—Å—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç? –ù—É –Ω–∞–¥–æ –∫–∞–∫-—Ç–æ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–∏—Ç—å —Å–±–æ—Ä —Å—Ç–∞—Ç–∏—Å—Ç–∏–∫–∏ –≤—Å—é–¥—É, –ø–æ –≤—Å–µ–º –º–µ—Å—Ç–∞–º, –≥–¥–µ –≤—ã–¥–µ–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–∞–º—è—Ç—å. –î–ª—è —Ç–∞–∫–æ–≥–æ —Ä–æ–¥–∞ –∑–∞–¥–∞—á –æ—Ç–ª–∏—á–Ω–æ –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥–∏—Ç –∞—Å–ø–µ–∫—Ç–Ω–æ-–æ—Ä–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ, –ª–∏–±–æ –ø—Ä—è–º–æ–µ –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –º–∞–Ω–∏–ø—É–ª—è—Ü–∏–π –±–∞–π—Ç-–∫–æ–¥–æ–º. (–¥–∞–ª–µ–µ –≤ —Å—Ç–∞—Ç—å–µ –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä –¥–æ–∫–ª–∞–¥–∞ –¥–µ–ª–∏—Ç—Å—è, –∫–∞–∫ —ç—Ç–æ –ª—É—á—à–µ –¥–µ–ª–∞—Ç—å)

–ö–æ–≥–¥–∞ –≤—ã –≤–≤–æ–¥–∏—Ç–µ –∞–¥—Ä–µ—Å —Å–∞–π—Ç–∞ –≤ –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–µ, –æ–Ω —Å–ø—Ä–∞—à–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç —É —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä–∞, —É—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω –ª–∏ –¥–ª—è —Å–∞–π—Ç–∞ —Å–µ—Ä—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç.
–í –æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –æ–±—â—É—é –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é –æ–± SSL-—Å–µ—Ä—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ç–µ –∏ –ø—É–±–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–π –∫–ª—é—á.
–ë—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä —Å–≤–µ—Ä—è–µ—Ç –∏–Ω—Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∞—Ü–∏—é —Å–æ —Å–ø–∏—Å–∫–æ–º –∞–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–∏–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Ü–µ–Ω—Ç—Ä–æ–≤ —Å–µ—Ä—Ç–∏—Ñ–∏–∫–∞—Ü–∏–∏. –¢–∞–∫–æ–π —Å–ø–∏—Å–æ–∫ –µ—Å—Ç—å –≤–æ –≤—Å–µ—Ö –ø–æ–ø—É–ª—è—Ä–Ω—ã—Ö –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä–∞—Ö.
–ï—Å–ª–∏ –≤—Å—ë –≤ –ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–∫–µ, –±—Ä–∞—É–∑–µ—Ä –≥–µ–Ω–µ—Ä–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç —Å–µ–∞–Ω—Å–æ–≤—ã–π –∫–ª—é—á, –∑–∞—à–∏—Ñ—Ä–æ–≤—ã–≤–∞–µ—Ç –µ–≥–æ –ø—É–±–ª–∏—á–Ω—ã–º –∫–ª—é—á–æ–º –∏ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –Ω–∞ —Å–µ—Ä–≤–µ—Ä.

–°–æ–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥—ã –≤ —Å–±–æ—Ä–∫–µ –º—É—Å–æ—Ä–∞ –≤ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∏—Ö Java (–∞–ª–≥–æ—Ä–∏—Ç–º—ã, –ø–∞–º—è—Ç—å –∏ —Ç.–ø.) üîó
https://www.baeldung.com/jvm-garbage-collectors
= Serial Garbage Collector
This is the simplest GC implementation, as it basically works with a single thread. As a result, this GC implementation freezes all application threads when it runs. Hence, it is not a good idea to use it in multi-threaded applications like server environments.
The Serial GC is the GC of choice for most applications that do not have small pause time requirements and run on client-style machines.
To enable Serial GC, we can use the following argument: -XX:+UseSerialGC

= Parallel Garbage Collector
It‚Äôs the default GC of the JVM and sometimes called Throughput Collector. Unlike Serial GC, this uses multiple threads for managing heap space. But it also freezes other application threads while performing GC.
If we use this GC, we can specify maximum garbage collection threads and pause time, throughput and footprint (heap size).
The numbers of garbage collector threads can be controlled with the command-line option -XX:ParallelGCThreads=.
The maximum pause time goal (gap [in milliseconds] between two GC) is specified with the command-line option -XX:MaxGCPauseMillis=.
The maximum throughput target (measured regarding the time spent doing garbage collection versus the time spent outside of garbage collection) is specified by the command-line option -XX:GCTimeRatio=.
Maximum heap footprint (the amount of heap memory that a program requires while running) is specified using the option -Xmx.
To enable Parallel GC, we can use the following argument: -XX:+UseParallelGC

= CMS Garbage Collector
The Concurrent Mark Sweep (CMS) implementation uses multiple garbage collector threads for garbage collection. It‚Äôs designed for applications that prefer shorter garbage collection pauses, and that can afford to share processor resources with the garbage collector while the application is running.
Simply put, applications using this type of GC respond slower on average but do not stop responding to perform garbage collection.
A quick point to note here is that since this GC is concurrent, an invocation of explicit garbage collection such as using System.gc() while the concurrent process is working, will result in Concurrent Mode Failure / Interruption.
If more than 98% of the total time is spent in CMS garbage collection and less than 2% of the heap is recovered, then an OutOfMemoryError is thrown by the CMS collector. If necessary, this feature can be disabled by adding the option -XX:-UseGCOverheadLimit to the command line.
This collector also has a mode knows as an incremental mode which is being deprecated in Java SE 8 and may be removed in a future major release.
To enable the CMS GC, we can use the following flag: -XX:+UseParNewGC

= G1 Garbage Collector
G1 (Garbage First) GC is designed for applications running on multi-processor machines with large memory space. It‚Äôs available since JDK7 Update 4 and in later releases.
G1 collector will replace the CMS collector since it‚Äôs more performance efficient.
Unlike other collectors, G1 collector partitions the heap into a set of equal-sized heap regions, each a contiguous range of virtual memory. When performing garbage collections, G1 shows a concurrent global marking phase (i.e. phase 1 known as Marking) to determine the liveness of objects throughout the heap.
After the mark phase is completed, G1 knows which regions are mostly empty. It collects in these areas first, which usually yields a significant amount of free space (i.e. phase 2 known as Sweeping). It is why this method of garbage collection is called Garbage-First.
To enable G1 GC, we can use the following argument: -XX:+UseG1GC

= News in Java 8
Java 8u20 has introduced one more JVM parameter for reducing the unnecessary use of memory by creating too many instances of same String. This optimizes the heap memory by removing duplicate String values to a global single char[] array.
This parameter can be enabled by adding -XX:+UseStringDeduplication as JVM parameter.

Root-aggregate philosophy üîó
https://deviq.com/aggregate-pattern/
An aggregate is a collection of one or more related entities (and possibly value objects). Each aggregate has a single root entity, referred to as the aggregate root. The aggregate root is responsible for controlling access to all of the members of its aggregate. It‚Äôs perfectly acceptable to single-entity aggregates, in which case that entity is itself the root of its aggregate. In addition to controlling access, the aggregate root is also responsible for ensuring the consistency of the aggregate. This is why it is important to ensure that the aggregate root does not directly expose its children, but rather controls access itself.
When applying the aggregate pattern, it is also important that persistence operations apply only at the aggregate root level. Thus, the aggregate root must be an entity, not a value object, so that it can be persisted to and from a data store using its ID. This is important, since it means the aggregate root can be certain that other parts of the system are not fetching its children, modifying them, and saving them without its knowledge. It also can simplify the relationships between entities, since typically navigation properties should only exist for types within aggregates, while other relationships should be by key only.
= As an example, consider an e-commerce domain which has concepts for Orders, which have multiple OrderItems, each of which refers to some quantity of Products being purchased. Adding and removing items to an Order should be controlled by the Order ‚Äì parts of the application shouldn‚Äôt be able to reach out and create an individual OrderItem as part of an Order without going through the Order. Deleting an Order should delete all of the OrderItems that are associated with it. So, Order makes sense as an aggregate root for the Order ‚Äì OrderItem group.
What about Product? Each OrderItem represents (among other things) a quantity of a product. Does it make sense for OrderItem to have a navigation property for Product? If so, that would complicate the Order aggregate, since ideally it should be able to traverse all of its navigation properties when persisting. As a test, does it make sense to delete Product A if an order for that product is deleted? Almost definitely not. Thus, Product doesn‚Äôt belong within the Order aggregate. It‚Äôs likely that Product should be its own aggregate root, in which case fetching product instances can be done using a Repository. All that‚Äôs required to do so is its ID. Thus, if OrderItem only refers to Product by Id, that‚Äôs sufficient.
In short (by mine words): we design app in such way, when entity grouped by domain spec and Order contains OrderItems, but OrderItem refers to particular Order by id only

–≠—Ç–æ—Ç –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å –¥–æ–ª–∂–µ–Ω –Ω–∞–º –Ω–∞–π—Ç–∏ –≤—Å–µ—Ö –∫–ª–∏–µ–Ω—Ç–æ–≤, —É –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö e-mail –∑–∞–∫–∞–Ω—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –Ω–∞ @yahoo.com, –æ–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –¥–∞–∂–µ –µ—Å–ª–∏ –ø–æ —Å—Ç–æ–ª–±—Ü—É email_address –µ—Å—Ç—å –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å, –°–£–ë–î –≤—Å—ë —Ä–∞–≤–Ω–æ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å –ø–æ–ª–Ω—ã–π –ø–µ—Ä–µ–±–æ—Ä —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã. –≠—Ç–æ —Å–≤—è–∑–∞–Ω–æ —Å —Ç–µ–º, —á—Ç–æ –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã —Å—Ç—Ä–æ—è—Ç—Å—è –≤ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ø–æ–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏–∏, —á—Ç–æ —Å–ª–æ–≤–∞/—Å–∏–º–≤–æ–ª—ã –∏–¥—É—Ç —Å–ª–µ–≤–∞ –Ω–∞–ø—Ä–∞–≤–æ. –ò—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ —Å–∏–º–≤–æ–ª–∞ –ø–æ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∫–∏ –≤ –Ω–∞—á–∞–ª–µ —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–∏—è –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞ –∏—Å–∫–ª—é—á–∞–µ—Ç –¥–ª—è –°–£–ë–î –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞ –ø–æ B-–¥–µ—Ä–µ–≤—É. –≠—Ç–∞ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º–∞ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å —Ä–µ—à–µ–Ω–∞ —Å–æ–∑–¥–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º –¥–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å–∞ –ø–æ –≤—ã—Ä–∞–∂–µ–Ω–∏—é reverse(email_address) –∏ —Ñ–æ—Ä–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ–º –∑–∞–ø—Ä–æ—Å–∞ –≤–∏–¥–∞: SELECT email_address FROM customers WHERE reverse(email_address) LIKE reverse('%@yahoo.com');.
–í –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–º —Å–ª—É—á–∞–µ —Å–∏–º–≤–æ–ª –ø–æ–¥—Å—Ç–∞–Ω–æ–≤–∫–∏ –æ–∫–∞–∂–µ—Ç—Å—è –≤ —Å–∞–º–æ–π –ø—Ä–∞–≤–æ–π –ø–æ–∑–∏—Ü–∏–∏ (moc.oohay@%), —á—Ç–æ –Ω–µ –∏—Å–∫–ª—é—á–∞–µ—Ç –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å–∞ –ø–æ reverse(email_address).

–ö–æ–º–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–Ω—ã–π –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å –≤ –ë–î üîó
–°–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–Ω–æ–π (–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ–∫–ª—é—á–µ–≤–æ–π, –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–Ω—ã–π) –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å ‚Äî —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∏—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–∏–º —Å—Ç–æ–ª–±—Ü–∞–º. –í–∞–∂–µ–Ω –ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–æ–∫ —Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø–æ–ª–µ–π
–¢–∞ –∂–µ —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, —á—Ç–æ –≤ –æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ–º –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å–µ, –Ω–æ –≤ —É–∑–ª–∞—Ö –ø—Ä–∏—Å—É—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—Ç –¥–æ–ø–æ–ª–Ω–∏—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–∏—è –¥–ª—è –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏—Ö —Å—Ç–æ–ª–±—Ü–æ–≤
–û–¥–∏–Ω –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–Ω—ã–π –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å –∑–∞–º–µ–Ω—è–µ—Ç –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –±–æ–ª–µ–µ –ø—Ä–æ—Å—Ç—ã—Ö: –∫ –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ—Ä—É –ø—Ä–∏ –Ω–∞–ª–∏—á–∏–∏ —Å–æ—Å—Ç–∞–≤–Ω–æ–≥–æ –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å–∞ –ø–æ –ê,–ë,–í —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–µ –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å—ã —É–∂–µ –Ω–µ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º—ã: –∏–Ω–¥–µ–∫—Å –ø–æ –ê; –∫–æ–º–ø–æ–∑–∏—Ç–Ω—ã–π –ø–æ –ê,–ë

–£—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–∏ –∏–∑–æ–ª—è—Ü–∏–∏ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–π, –Ω–∞–∑–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –æ–Ω–∏ —Ä–µ—à–∞—é—Ç. –∫–∞–∫–æ–π —É—Ä–æ–≤–µ–Ω—å –ø–æ —É–º–æ–ª—á–∞–Ω–∏—é? üîó

–ü—Ä–∏ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–ª–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–º –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–π –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω—ã —Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–µ –ø—Ä–æ–±–ª–µ–º—ã:
= –ø–æ—Ç–µ—Ä—è–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–µ (lost update) ‚Äî –ø—Ä–∏ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≤—Ä–µ–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–º –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–≥–æ –±–ª–æ–∫–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã–º–∏ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏—è–º–∏ —Ç–µ—Ä—è—é—Ç—Å—è –≤—Å–µ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è, –∫—Ä–æ–º–µ –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–µ–≥–æ;
= "–≥—Ä—è–∑–Ω–æ–µ" —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–µ (dirty read) ‚Äî —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –∏–ª–∏ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω—ë–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–µ–π, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–∞—è –≤–ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥—Å—Ç–≤–∏–∏ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–¥—Ç–≤–µ—Ä–¥–∏—Ç—Å—è (–æ—Ç–∫–∞—Ç–∏—Ç—Å—è);
= –Ω–µ–ø–æ–≤—Ç–æ—Ä—è—é—â–µ–µ—Å—è —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–µ (non-repeatable read) ‚Äî –ø—Ä–∏ –ø–æ–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω–æ–º —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–∏ –≤ —Ä–∞–º–∫–∞—Ö –æ–¥–Ω–æ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏ —Ä–∞–Ω–µ–µ –ø—Ä–æ—á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –æ–∫–∞–∑—ã–≤–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω—ë–Ω–Ω—ã–º–∏;
= —Ñ–∞–Ω—Ç–æ–º–Ω–æ–µ —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–µ (phantom reads) ‚Äî –æ–¥–Ω–∞ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏—è –≤ —Ö–æ–¥–µ —Å–≤–æ–µ–≥–æ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —Ä–∞–∑ –≤—ã–±–∏—Ä–∞–µ—Ç –º–Ω–æ–∂–µ—Å—Ç–≤–æ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫ –ø–æ –æ–¥–Ω–∏–º –∏ —Ç–µ–º –∂–µ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∏—è–º. –î—Ä—É–≥–∞—è —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏—è –≤ –∏–Ω—Ç–µ—Ä–≤–∞–ª–∞—Ö –º–µ–∂–¥—É —ç—Ç–∏–º–∏ –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä–∫–∞–º–∏ –¥–æ–±–∞–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç –∏–ª–∏ —É–¥–∞–ª—è–µ—Ç —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∏ –∏–ª–∏ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω—è–µ—Ç —Å—Ç–æ–ª–±—Ü—ã –Ω–µ–∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫, –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É–µ–º—ã—Ö –≤ –∫—Ä–∏—Ç–µ—Ä–∏—è—Ö –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä–∫–∏ –ø–µ—Ä–≤–æ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏, –∏ —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–æ –∑–∞–∫–∞–Ω—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è. –í —Ä–µ–∑—É–ª—å—Ç–∞—Ç–µ –ø–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—Å—è, —á—Ç–æ –æ–¥–Ω–∏ –∏ —Ç–µ –∂–µ –≤—ã–±–æ—Ä–∫–∏ –≤ –ø–µ—Ä–≤–æ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –¥–∞—é—Ç —Ä–∞–∑–Ω—ã–µ –º–Ω–æ–∂–µ—Å—Ç–≤–∞ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫.

–ü–æ–¥ "—É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ–º –∏–∑–æ–ª—è—Ü–∏–∏ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–π" –ø–æ–Ω–∏–º–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è —Å—Ç–µ–ø–µ–Ω—å –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏–≤–∞–µ–º–æ–π –≤–Ω—É—Ç—Ä–µ–Ω–Ω–∏–º–∏ –º–µ—Ö–∞–Ω–∏–∑–º–∞–º–∏ –°–£–ë–î (—Ç–æ –µ—Å—Ç—å –Ω–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–±—É—é—â–µ–π —Å–ø–µ—Ü–∏–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–≥–æ –ø—Ä–æ–≥—Ä–∞–º–º–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è) –∑–∞—â–∏—Ç—ã –æ—Ç –≤—Å–µ—Ö –∏–ª–∏ –Ω–µ–∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö –≤—ã—à–µ–ø–µ—Ä–µ—á–∏—Å–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –≤–∏–¥–æ–≤ –Ω–µ—Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –≤–æ–∑–Ω–∏–∫–∞—é—â–∏—Ö –ø—Ä–∏ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–ª–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–º –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–∏ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–π. –°—Ç–∞–Ω–¥–∞—Ä—Ç SQL-92 –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª—è–µ—Ç —à–∫–∞–ª—É –∏–∑ —á–µ—Ç—ã—Ä—ë—Ö —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ–π –∏–∑–æ–ª—è—Ü–∏–∏: Read uncommitted, Read committed, Repeatable read, Serializable. –ü–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π –∏–∑ –Ω–∏—Ö —è–≤–ª—è–µ—Ç—Å—è —Å–∞–º—ã–º —Å–ª–∞–±—ã–º, –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–Ω–∏–π ‚Äî —Å–∞–º—ã–º —Å–∏–ª—å–Ω—ã–º, –∫–∞–∂–¥—ã–π –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥—É—é—â–∏–π –≤–∫–ª—é—á–∞–µ—Ç –≤ —Å–µ–±—è –≤—Å–µ –ø—Ä–µ–¥—ã–¥—É—â–∏–µ.

= Read uncommitted (—á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–µ–∑–∞—Ñ–∏–∫—Å–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö)
–ù–∏–∑—à–∏–π (–ø–µ—Ä–≤—ã–π) —É—Ä–æ–≤–µ–Ω—å –∏–∑–æ–ª—è—Ü–∏–∏. –û–Ω –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –æ—Ç—Å—É—Ç—Å—Ç–≤–∏–µ –ø–æ—Ç–µ—Ä—è–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –æ–±–Ω–æ–≤–ª–µ–Ω–∏–π. –ï—Å–ª–∏ –Ω–µ—Å–∫–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–ª–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–π –ø—ã—Ç–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω—è—Ç—å –æ–¥–Ω—É –∏ —Ç—É –∂–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫—É —Ç–∞–±–ª–∏—Ü—ã, —Ç–æ –≤ –æ–∫–æ–Ω—á–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ–º –≤–∞—Ä–∏–∞–Ω—Ç–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∞ –±—É–¥–µ—Ç –∏–º–µ—Ç—å –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –æ–ø—Ä–µ–¥–µ–ª–µ–Ω–Ω–æ–µ –≤—Å–µ–º –Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä–æ–º —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–æ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–π. –ü—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º –≤–æ–∑–º–æ–∂–Ω–æ —Å—á–∏—Ç—ã–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ –Ω–µ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –ª–æ–≥–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –Ω–µ—Å–æ–≥–ª–∞—Å–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –Ω–æ –∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã—Ö –µ—â—ë –Ω–µ –∑–∞—Ñ–∏–∫—Å–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã.
–¢–∏–ø–∏—á–Ω—ã–π —Å–ø–æ—Å–æ–± —Ä–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω—è –∏–∑–æ–ª—è—Ü–∏–∏ ‚Äî –±–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∞ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –Ω–∞ –≤—Ä–µ–º—è –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ã –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è, —á—Ç–æ –≥–∞—Ä–∞–Ω—Ç–∏—Ä—É–µ—Ç, —á—Ç–æ –∫–æ–º–∞–Ω–¥—ã –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –æ–¥–Ω–∏—Ö –∏ —Ç–µ—Ö –∂–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫, –∑–∞–ø—É—â–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–ª–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ, —Ñ–∞–∫—Ç–∏—á–µ—Å–∫–∏ –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è—é—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ, –∏ –Ω–∏ –æ–¥–Ω–æ –∏–∑ –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–π –Ω–µ –ø–æ—Ç–µ—Ä—è–µ—Ç—Å—è. –¢—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏, –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è—é—â–∏–µ —Ç–æ–ª—å–∫–æ —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–µ, –ø—Ä–∏ –¥–∞–Ω–Ω–æ–º —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ –∏–∑–æ–ª—è—Ü–∏–∏ –Ω–∏–∫–æ–≥–¥–∞ –Ω–µ –±–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä—É—é—Ç—Å—è.

= Read committed (—á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏–µ —Ñ–∏–∫—Å–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö) (–æ–Ω –æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ - –ø–æ —É–º–æ–ª—á–∞–Ω–∏—é)
–ë–æ–ª—å—à–∏–Ω—Å—Ç–≤–æ –ø—Ä–æ–º—ã—à–ª–µ–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö –°–£–ë–î, –≤ —á–∞—Å—Ç–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏, Microsoft SQL Server, PostgreSQL –∏ Oracle, –ø–æ —É–º–æ–ª—á–∞–Ω–∏—é –∏—Å–ø–æ–ª—å–∑—É—é—Ç –∏–º–µ–Ω–Ω–æ —ç—Ç–æ—Ç —É—Ä–æ–≤–µ–Ω—å. –ù–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–º —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ –æ–±–µ—Å–ø–µ—á–∏–≤–∞–µ—Ç—Å—è –∑–∞—â–∏—Ç–∞ –æ—Ç —á–µ—Ä–Ω–æ–≤–æ–≥–æ, "–≥—Ä—è–∑–Ω–æ–≥–æ" —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏—è, —Ç–µ–º –Ω–µ –º–µ–Ω–µ–µ, –≤ –ø—Ä–æ—Ü–µ—Å—Å–µ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã –æ–¥–Ω–æ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∞—è –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –±—ã—Ç—å —É—Å–ø–µ—à–Ω–æ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∞ –∏ —Å–¥–µ–ª–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ –µ—é –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –∑–∞—Ñ–∏–∫—Å–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã. –í –∏—Ç–æ–≥–µ –ø–µ—Ä–≤–∞—è —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏—è –±—É–¥–µ—Ç —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞—Ç—å —Å –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–º –Ω–∞–±–æ—Ä–æ–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö.
–†–µ–∞–ª–∏–∑–∞—Ü–∏—è –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à—ë–Ω–Ω–æ–≥–æ —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏—è –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤—ã–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –Ω–∞ –æ–¥–Ω–æ–º –∏–∑ –¥–≤—É—Ö –ø–æ–¥—Ö–æ–¥–æ–≤: –±–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–∏ –∏–ª–∏ –≤–µ—Ä—Å–∏–æ–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏.

= Repeatable read (–ø–æ–≤—Ç–æ—Ä—è–µ–º–æ—Å—Ç—å —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏—è)
–£—Ä–æ–≤–µ–Ω—å, –ø—Ä–∏ –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä–æ–º —á–∏—Ç–∞—é—â–∞—è —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏—è ¬´–Ω–µ –≤–∏–¥–∏—Ç¬ª –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω–µ–Ω–∏—è –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã—Ö, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –±—ã–ª–∏ –µ—é —Ä–∞–Ω–µ–µ –ø—Ä–æ—á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω—ã. –ü—Ä–∏ —ç—Ç–æ–º –Ω–∏–∫–∞–∫–∞—è –¥—Ä—É–≥–∞—è —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏—è –Ω–µ –º–æ–∂–µ—Ç –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω—è—Ç—å –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–µ, —á–∏—Ç–∞–µ–º—ã–µ —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–µ–π, –ø–æ–∫–∞ —Ç–∞ –Ω–µ –æ–∫–æ–Ω—á–µ–Ω–∞.
–ë–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∏ –≤ —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª—è—é—â–µ–º —Ä–µ–∂–∏–º–µ –ø—Ä–∏–º–µ–Ω—è—é—Ç—Å—è –∫–æ –≤—Å–µ–º –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º, —Å—á–∏—Ç—ã–≤–∞–µ–º—ã–º –ª—é–±–æ–π –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ü–∏–µ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏, –∏ —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—è—é—Ç—Å—è –¥–æ –µ—ë –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∏—è. –≠—Ç–æ –∑–∞–ø—Ä–µ—â–∞–µ—Ç –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–º —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏—è–º –∏–∑–º–µ–Ω—è—Ç—å —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∏, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–µ –±—ã–ª–∏ —Å—á–∏—Ç–∞–Ω—ã –Ω–µ–∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à—ë–Ω–Ω–æ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–µ–π. –û–¥–Ω–∞–∫–æ –¥—Ä—É–≥–∏–µ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –º–æ–≥—É—Ç –≤—Å—Ç–∞–≤–ª—è—Ç—å –Ω–æ–≤—ã–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∏, —Å–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—â–∏–µ —É—Å–ª–æ–≤–∏—è–º –ø–æ–∏—Å–∫–∞ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ü–∏–π, —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞—â–∏—Ö—Å—è –≤ —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏. –ü—Ä–∏ –ø–æ–≤—Ç–æ—Ä–Ω–æ–º –∑–∞–ø—É—Å–∫–µ –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ü–∏–∏ —Ç–µ–∫—É—â–µ–π —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–µ–π –±—É–¥—É—Ç –∏–∑–≤–ª–µ—á–µ–Ω—ã –Ω–æ–≤—ã–µ —Å—Ç—Ä–æ–∫–∏, —á—Ç–æ –ø—Ä–∏–≤–µ–¥—ë—Ç –∫ —Ñ–∞–Ω—Ç–æ–º–Ω–æ–º—É —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏—é. –£—á–∏—Ç—ã–≤–∞—è —Ç–æ, —á—Ç–æ —Ä–∞–∑–¥–µ–ª—è—é—â–∏–µ –±–ª–æ–∫–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∫–∏ —Å–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω—è—é—Ç—Å—è –¥–æ –∑–∞–≤–µ—Ä—à–µ–Ω–∏—è —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏, –∞ –Ω–µ —Å–Ω–∏–º–∞—é—Ç—Å—è –≤ –∫–æ–Ω—Ü–µ –∫–∞–∂–¥–æ–π –∏–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ü–∏–∏, —Å—Ç–µ–ø–µ–Ω—å –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–ª–µ–ª–∏–∑–º–∞ –Ω–∏–∂–µ, —á–µ–º –ø—Ä–∏ —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ –∏–∑–æ–ª—è—Ü–∏–∏ READ COMMITTED. –ü–æ—ç—Ç–æ–º—É –ø–æ–ª—å–∑–æ–≤–∞—Ç—å—Å—è –¥–∞–Ω–Ω—ã–º –∏ –±–æ–ª–µ–µ –≤—ã—Å–æ–∫–∏–º–∏ —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω—è–º–∏ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–π –±–µ–∑ –Ω–µ–æ–±—Ö–æ–¥–∏–º–æ—Å—Ç–∏ –æ–±—ã—á–Ω–æ –Ω–µ —Ä–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥—É–µ—Ç—Å—è.

= Serializable (—É–ø–æ—Ä—è–¥–æ—á–∏–≤–∞–µ–º–æ—Å—Ç—å)
–°–∞–º—ã–π –≤—ã—Å–æ–∫–∏–π —É—Ä–æ–≤–µ–Ω—å –∏–∑–æ–ª–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–Ω–æ—Å—Ç–∏; —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–æ–ª–Ω–æ—Å—Ç—å—é –∏–∑–æ–ª–∏—Ä—É—é—Ç—Å—è –¥—Ä—É–≥ –æ—Ç –¥—Ä—É–≥–∞, –∫–∞–∂–¥–∞—è –≤—ã–ø–æ–ª–Ω—è–µ—Ç—Å—è –ø–æ—Å–ª–µ–¥–æ–≤–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω–æ, –∫–∞–∫ –±—É–¥—Ç–æ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–ª–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã—Ö —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–π –Ω–µ —Å—É—â–µ—Å—Ç–≤—É–µ—Ç. –¢–æ–ª—å–∫–æ –Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–º —É—Ä–æ–≤–Ω–µ –ø–∞—Ä–∞–ª–ª–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∑–∞–∫—Ü–∏–∏ –Ω–µ –ø–æ–¥–≤–µ—Ä–∂–µ–Ω—ã —ç—Ñ—Ñ–µ–∫—Ç—É "—Ñ–∞–Ω—Ç–æ–º–Ω–æ–≥–æ —á—Ç–µ–Ω–∏—è"
